Main Points of the Japanese Government's Opinion 56

Formally Announced by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs

Slander of Our Republic Unbearable to Read

Our Country's Authorities Should Refute Strongly

▲ Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 20th. The following are the main points of the Imperial Government's opinion on the Lytton Report submitted to the League of Nations, which was officially announced by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at noon on the 21st.

▲ Introduction. The Imperial Government expresses gratitude for the efforts of the investigation team, but due to the short duration of the investigation, the impressions gained by the committee members are superficial. It is regrettable that the team did not visit South China, as this is reflected in the report's lack of optimism. While the report was undoubtedly written in good faith, the selection and collection of materials presented to the committee members is perceived as flawed. It clearly relies on newspaper articles, personal correspondence, and private conversations. It is difficult to determine the value of this evidence, which is used only when it is unfavorable to Japan, especially in regards to the September 18th Incident and the establishment of Manchukuo. In the former case, the motives of the Japanese military's actions are fundamentally misunderstood. In the latter case, the future of Manchukuo's rule is inconsistent with the main points of other parts of the report and with actual events. Finally, the report implies that the Japanese hold deep resentment towards the Chinese people, which is contrary to the facts. Japan hopes for everlasting friendship between the two countries.

▲ Chapter 1: China. Chapter 1 on China is divided into three sections: 1) General Observations, 2) Anti-Foreign Activities in China, and 3) Anomalous Status of Foreigners in China. 1) General Observations: China is not a unified nation. 2) The Nationalist Government promotes anti-foreign education, bearing the responsibility for resistance. The Kuomintang, i.e. the Nationalist Government, should be held responsible, with Japan being the biggest victim. 3) Anomalous Status of Foreigners in China: Foreign powers have extraterritorial rights in China, as well as police and administrative power in concessions in Dalian, Hankou, Shanghai, and other areas. They directly protect their rights with armed force by stationing necessary troops. It is stated that this special status is difficult to apply to a nation like China, even with current peace mechanisms.

▲ Chapter 2: Manchukuo. Chapter 2 on Manchukuo is divided into four sections: 1) General Observations, 2) Zhang Family's Misrule, 3) Japan's Special Status, and 4) Infringement of Japan's Status. 1) General Observations: Points out that Manchuria has never been fully part of China. 2) Describes the Zhang family's misrule in Manchuria. 3) Emphasizes Japan's special status in Manchuria and Japan's cultural achievements. 4) Describes China's infringement of Japan's status, citing China's encirclement policy against the South Manchurian Railway as severely hindering the exercise of commercial lease rights and other treaty rights, oppressing Japanese citizens, especially Koreans in Manchuria, and the Nakamura Incident. It is argued that the Chinese side's attitude of attacking Japan and the bombing incident on September 18th were not without cause.

▲ Chapter 3: The September 18th Incident and Subsequent Military Actions. Chapter 3 describes the September 18th Incident and subsequent military actions, stating that the Japanese military's actions did not exceed the scope of any self-defense. The Imperial Government does not allow external discussion of whether the actions were necessary or appropriate.

▲ Chapter 4: The New State. Chapter 4 is divided into three sections, A, B, and C. A, states that the establishment of Manchukuo and the independence movement of Manchukuo were directed and assisted by the Tokyo General Staff Headquarters, which is completely contrary to the facts. It states that the Japanese side did not participate in the independence movement. B, Concerns the attitude of the people of Manchukuo, listing 1,550 letters from Chinese people whose identities are unknown, and stating that many letters express dissatisfaction. It also states that the people of Manchukuo continue to welcome the new government. C, Concerns the organization of Manchukuo and its future, drawing particular attention to the restoration of security and finance. It refutes the misjudgment that Japan controls Manchukuo and points out that no provision in the Japan-Manchukuo Protocol violates any international obligation.

▲ Chapter 5: Conclusion. The above sections are summarized as follows: 1) China is nearly in a state of anarchy and chaos. If this situation continues, it is nothing less than the collapse of the national entity. However, it is difficult to predict whether a strong and permanent central government will ultimately emerge. 2) As a result, China cannot adequately protect the lives and property of foreigners, especially with the intensification of internal strife and the so-called revolutionary diplomacy. 3) However, foreign powers continue to exercise extraterritorial rights, concessions, and the stationing of troops, as well as the unique practice of permanent warships on inland rivers, continuing unprecedented exceptional powers and privileges. 4) Japan is the biggest victim of China's anarchic state and anti-foreign policy. 5) Japan and Manchuria have close historical and geographical ties, with enormous economic interests and significant treaty rights in the region. At the same time, there are also a large number of residents, and from the perspective of national security, Manchuria has significant political and strategic importance. In the end, Japan's status in Manchuria is unparalleled and exceptionally special. 6) Old Manchurian officials attempted to reverse the aforementioned special status, especially after Zhang Xueliang's approach to the Nationalist Government, resulting in frequent and fierce infringements on Japanese rights and interests. Although Japan has made efforts to ease this situation, it has led to this tense situation. 7) The actions taken by the Japanese military during the September 18th Incident, in that urgent atmosphere, or thereafter, did not exceed the scope of self-defense. From a fair perspective, other countries would have taken the same actions under the same conditions. 8) Manchuria is geographically and historically separate from mainland China. Its residents resent the Zhang family's tyranny and oppose dragging Manchuria into the vortex of China's internal political struggles. The idea of establishing Manchukuo is based on this "protecting the territory and pacifying the people" movement and the spontaneous actions of Manchurian residents, with the Qing Dynasty restoration movement as the main driving force. Manchukuo is making steady progress under a stable policy, and its future is very promising.

Finally, Japan's attitude towards the construction of Manchukuo and formal recognition does not violate any international treaty. What needs to be emphasized further is that the complexity of the China problem is even greater than that of the Manchurian problem. Its anomalous characteristics are unparalleled. It is more difficult to handle this situation with the general formulas applicable to ordinary international problems. The procedures for resolving such anomalous problems cannot be based on precedents commonly applicable to international disputes, as the report states.

Regarding the China problem, the above is based on the Imperial Government's basic view of the points written in Chapters 9 and 10 of the report. The report rejects the restoration of the status quo ante and also considers the maintenance of the current regime to be an unsatisfactory solution. The Imperial Government believes that such a solution does not violate the fundamental principles of international obligations, is consistent with the hopes of the people of Manchuria, and is confident that this solution is the only foundation for stabilizing Sino-Japanese relations. If the new nation, which is developing strongly, is dissolved, it will be placed in international isolation. What the report calls "not suitable for the realities of the situation" means that Japan's relationship with Manchukuo cannot be abandoned to a state of perpetual instability. Therefore, the Imperial Government hopes that the countries will quickly recognize Manchukuo and cooperate to make its development stable and that the situation in Manchuria will be peaceful in the Far East, which is the only way. This is why Japan signed the agreement on September 15th. The report states that the situation has not stopped, which is a profound meaning of the characteristics of the Manchurian problem. The Council of Directors should refer to the opinions of the committee and review the report, hoping to obtain full understanding and satisfactory information about the subsequent situation, which is constantly changing. The changes in the situation in mainland China remain chaotic, while Manchukuo is gradually moving towards development. The Imperial Government is always prepared to provide this information. Among the proposals for solutions in Chapter 10, it is recommended that China and Japan negotiate directly, stating that this is not the function of the committee. This proposal only signifies one example of how to implement the principles of Chapter 9. Japan said that it would quickly recognize Manchukuo, believing that Japan's recognition might somewhat obscure the importance of the proposal. Because the committee once said that even if Japan recognizes the new nation, it may be effective in the report, but it issued it in vague words, so Japan made the above statement. From the above point of view, the Imperial Government's view is: 1) As mentioned later, Principle 10 in Chapter 9 of the report, I am afraid it will involve the international management of mainland China. Similarly, in Chapter 10, regarding the proposals on Manchuria, if implemented, it will call for the disguised international management of Manchuria, which is difficult for both Manchukuo and Japan to accept. 2) This proposal is too precise and complicated and does not fit the realities of the Far East situation. The case put forward by the committee must have a consolidated and stable central government of the warring country as the minimum prerequisite. If the Manchurian problem has no precedent and is complicated, however, if one of the ruling countries does not have a consolidated and trustworthy central government, it will only complicate the situation. 3) Abolishing the military preparedness of Manchuria, such as using international police forces to maintain peace and order, etc., must be regarded as completely inconsistent with the realities of the situation. This is difficult to live up to the hopes of the residents of Manchuria, and at the same time, it is feared that it will cause the unrest and chaos in the area that Japan wants to prevent. This is a greater deterioration of the situation than restoring the status quo. If you talk about the abstract principles in Chapter 9, it is clear that they cannot be applied if China does not have a strong central government. Therefore, in the current state of continued anarchy, it is impossible to resolve these problems without international cooperation, and it is impossible to realize a strong central government. This international cooperation can hardly be imagined without any form of international management. Japan cannot wait for China's reconstruction, because for the reasons mentioned above, the peace and order that is now on the road to restoration is in danger of being destroyed, so no matter what the case is, it will call for new disputes and difficulties. However, is the effort to stabilize the situation in Manchuria truly managed? The world, which has shown so much patience and sympathy for China's re-emergence over the past two decades, welcomes those who have understanding and hope for the new nation in Manchuria? Also, the major Chinese problem is greatly simplified by its own solution.

British King Congratulates Amy Johnson by Telegram 62

Amy Sleeps Soundly for Fifteen Hours

Telegrams of Congratulations Arrive Like Snowflakes from Various Countries

▲ Reuters, London, 19th – According to a cable from Cape Town, telegrams congratulating Amy Johnson on her successful flight are pouring in from all over the world. Today, after sleeping soundly for fifteen hours, the female aviator first received a telegram from the British King congratulating her on her success and inquiring about her well-being. Subsequently, the British Minister of Aviation, the British Aviation Club, and world-renowned aviators such as Miss Earhart, the female aviator who flew across the Atlantic alone, and the Frenchman Costes, all sent telegrams of congratulations. London received Amy's radio broadcast stating that she chose the southern route to test her own endurance. She had never flown continuously day and night without rest before, and she was not sure if she could do it this time. She now feels refreshed and is ready to fly back to England. Her husband, Morrison, said after speaking to Amy on the phone today that Amy might plan to fly back to England from Cape Town, setting a new record, but he thought it was unlikely.

▲ Forcing Legal Groups in Three Provinces to Falsely Attest to Public Opinion

Beiping Correspondence: Recently, the Japanese side has been spreading propaganda in the northern part of Manchuria, claiming that they are conducting peace negotiations with Su Bingwen, Commander-in-Chief of the Heilongjiang National Salvation Army, and that the war in northern Manchuria will be resolved peacefully. Furthermore, the Lytton Report stated that the establishment of Manchukuo was not based on public opinion. Therefore, the Japanese side specially sent commissioners to the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang to force legal groups in each province to issue certificates supporting the puppet state, intending to deceive the League of Nations. Su Bingwen sent a telegram to Beiping on the cold day (the 14th) reporting that the Japanese side had repeatedly telegraphed seeking peace, but had been rejected. The two of us have long been friends with you, and we believe you know that we are open-minded. Therefore, we will certainly do our best for you. We hope you will understand our sincerity and not doubt it. We hope you will agree to a prompt negotiation and inform us of the name of your representative. Komatsubara, Head of the Japanese Special Service Agency in Harbin, kowtows. 3. Telegram from Harbin: To Commander-in-Chief Han. Today, Chief Komatsubara of the Japanese Special Service Agency has been dispatched as the plenipotentiary representative of the Commander of the Kwantung Army to the 86th small station on the Russian border to negotiate directly with you and explain all previous misunderstandings. It has been verified that Colonel Komatsubara admires you the most and sympathizes with all your colleagues. Ji and others have been ordered to accompany him for negotiations. We will do our best to protect your personality and find ways to relieve your suffering, with the premise of resolving the dispute as soon as possible. You have always loved the people of Hailun and Manchuria. At this time, when the people are suffering from hunger and cold, we believe you will think of them and come to their rescue. If the hearts of the people of Hailun and Manchuria are not settled, and it is inconvenient for you to leave, please select a senior official to go for a face-to-face meeting. We sincerely pray. Wang Ji and Shao Lin kowtow. 4. Telegram from Bukui: To Commander-in-Chief Han. It is true that Colonel Komatsubara has set off for Daulia. Lin and others are allowed to pass over Hailun-Manzhouli tomorrow. No matter what your opinions are, please send someone to Manchuria for negotiation. Lin and others will do their best to seek peace. Our humble hearts hope to be accepted. Shao Lin and Wang Ji kowtow with seals. 5. Komatsubara took a plane and crossed the sea to the Matishaizi station. It is also heard that the Japanese side is spreading to the Soviet Union that the Japanese side dispatched personnel to negotiate at our request. 6. Shao Lin and others also took two planes across the sea to Russia on the cold day. 7. After investigating the Japanese side's telegrams requesting peace, we have not paid any attention to them, fearing confusion. According to reliable reports, because the Lytton Report stated that the establishment of Manchukuo was not based on public opinion, Chief of Staff Koiso of the Kwantung Army came to Jiang on Dong (the 1st) and forced legal groups in various counties to issue certificates supporting Manchukuo. These certificates have been fabricated and handed over by Han Yunjie, the puppet governor. It is heard that the provinces of Fengtian and Jilin have also adopted similar methods. After investigating the Japanese people's actions, the original intention was to deceive the League of Nations. If we do not clarify and expose the secrets, we are deeply afraid that rumors will spread far and wide, confusing the true with the false. Please make every effort to correct this and clarify the truth. We look forward to hearing more news. Su Bingwen kowtows with a cold seal."

Provisional Law on Supervising Local Finances Passed by the Legislative Yuan 65

The Legislative Yuan passed the Provisional Law on Supervising Local Finances at its morning meeting on the 19th. The original text is as follows: (Article 1) The supervision of local finances throughout the country shall be carried out in accordance with the provisions of this Law. (Article 2) The supervisory agency for financial administration at all levels of local finances shall be the Ministry of Finance, unless otherwise provided by law. (Article 3) When each province and municipality directly under the Executive Yuan plans to change tax categories, increase or decrease tax rates, or raise public bonds, the provincial or municipal government shall, in accordance with the law, prepare a plan, consult with the Ministry of Finance for review and endorsement, and submit it to the Executive Yuan for transfer to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation and resolution, and submit it to the National Government for promulgation. (Article 4) Counties and cities shall not change tax categories unless required by law. When there is an increase or decrease in tax rates or the raising of public bonds, the county or city government shall, in accordance with the law, prepare a plan and convene local legal groups for public discussion before the establishment of the county or city council, and submit it to the Finance Department for review, endorsement, and submission to the provincial government for deliberation and promulgation, and send it to the Ministry of Finance for record. (Article 5) Local governments at all levels shall not collect taxes in advance or establish new surcharges, which shall be regarded as increasing tax rates. (Article 6) Local governments at all levels shall not apply to levy the following types of taxes, which have harmful effects: (1) those that harm the public interest of society; (2) those that harm the source of central government revenue; (3) double taxation; (4) those that hinder transportation; (5) taxation that unfairly favors the import of goods from one locality over another for the benefit of one locality; (6) transit taxes on goods passing through various localities. (Article 7) Local governments at all levels shall not implement changes in tax categories, increases or decreases in tax rates, or the raising of public bonds without approval in accordance with the provisions of Articles 3 and 4 of this Law, and shall not include them in the budget. (Article 8) The division of taxation between the central and local governments shall be determined by law in accordance with the provisions of Article 61 of the Provisional Constitution. (Article 9) The Finance Departments of each province and the Finance Bureaus of municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan shall report the financial situation and actual revenue and expenditure of the province or municipality to the Ministry of Finance, the Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics, and the Ministry of Audit for verification on a monthly basis. The financial situation and actual revenue and expenditure of each county and city shall be compiled by the Finance Department at the end of each fiscal year and reported to the Ministry of Finance, the Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics, and the Ministry of Audit for verification. (Article 10) This Law shall come into force on the date of its promulgation.

▲ Zhang Gang's Bandits, Si Shun, Were Defeated

▲ Bandits in Dongkeng Were Also Eliminated

Our 5th Regiment moved to Shicheng on the 15th." (November 16th)

Jingdezhen Porcelain Industry Plummets 69

▲ External Dumping of Foreign Porcelain, Internal Heavy Taxes and Fees

▲ Porcelain Merchants Gasping for Breath, Increasing Number of Unemployed Workers

Nanchang Correspondence: Jingdezhen's porcelain is the only special product of our country and is extremely famous in the world. Jingdezhen was formerly known as Changnan. In the early Tang Dynasty, Huo Zhongchu, a native of Dongshanli, and Tao Yu, a town resident, made porcelain called "fake jade," which was a tribute and not easily available to the people. It was not until Jingde years of the Song Dynasty that the town was established and renamed its current name, becoming the first industrial area in our country. Since then, special officials have been set up in all dynasties to manage it, such as the Jingde Kiln and Xianghu Kiln in the Song Dynasty, the Longwan Kiln in the Ming Dynasty, and the Imperial Kiln in the Qing Dynasty, which were carefully studied and imitated, and inventions were made in each generation. It was sold to Europe and the United States, and together with silk and tea, it was a major export product of our country. However, due to the simple knowledge of the workers, they were conservative and did not know how to improve. The quality of the products deteriorated. The authorities did not promote or improve, and the taxes and fees were added repeatedly, and the cost increased day by day, so that foreign porcelain took the opportunity to enter. Not only was the international market squeezed out and had no foothold, but also the domestic sales were usurped, with a great tendency to become the master. It is found that in the prosperous era of porcelain in Jingdezhen in the early Qing Dynasty, there were about 150,000 to 180,000 workers, with the saying "thousands of pigs and ten thousand rice," that is, the number of pigs needed per day was thousands and the number of rice consumed was ten thousand dan. The total value of porcelain products each year was always more than ten million. According to the survey of the Construction Department in the 18th year of the Republic of China, there were a total of 1,284 factories and 144 porcelain kilns in the town. The total capital of the kiln households was about 1,369,234 yuan. The output of that year, which can be counted, was: 823,910 yuan for gray ware, 65,518 yuan for large ware, 11,900 yuan for lamp stands, 184,250 yuan for antique ware, 246,345 yuan for carving, 57,380 yuan for official lids, 586,578 yuan for pink fixing, 18,800 yuan for light tracing, 27,820 yuan for talc, 73,900 yuan for tracing jars, 56,607 yuan for small ware, and 317,460 yuan for large pieces, totaling more than 2.4 million yuan. This number is determined from tax revenue statistics, and of course it is not very accurate. According to general estimates, the total value of porcelain products in that year (the 18th year) was about 4 million to 5 million yuan, which is no match for the millions in the heyday. Recently, porcelain merchants from Jingdezhen talked about the porcelain industry in Jingdezhen, which has been affected by foreign porcelain in recent years, and exports have decreased. The capital has been unable to turn around. The town was captured by Fang Zhimin's bandits two years ago, and the essence of the town was swept away. Whether kiln households or porcelain merchants were all gasping for breath. Fortunately, sales started in February and March last year (the town has always regarded May, July, August and September as peak months, and the rest as off-season months). Various gangs in Shanghai, Tianjin, Guangzhou, and Hong Kong competed to purchase and pre-prepared foreign goods. However, after the September 18th Incident, business became deserted again. Porcelain merchants hoped that there would be a turnaround this year, but the Shanghai war broke out and no one cared about it. Large capital could barely turn around, but small capital could not borrow and support was difficult, and they closed down one after another. After the Shanghai war stopped, there could have been a turnaround, but the production and sales tax was levied at this time, and a glimmer of hope was cut off from then on. This production and sales tax is based on the precedent of the previous production and sales tax, mostly 10%, that is, one-tenth of the tax rate is already heavy, and the cost will naturally be high, and sales will also be cut off accordingly. Therefore, the entire town's industry and commerce unanimously opposed it, and the entire city's closure lasted for nearly a week. Fortunately, the garrison did not cause an accident, but the production and sales tax bureau still disregarded everything and detained all the porcelain that was unloaded. Porcelain merchants hesitated, and kiln households and factories all stopped. Although the National Porcelain Industry Association appealed to the central government to issue an order to cancel it, the authorities ignored it and still collect it, so the entire town's porcelain industry has been closed for several months. Although work has resumed now, the 100 or so kilns, which used to be fired every five days, are now changed to once every 18 days, but the goods are still piled up like mountains, and every household has nowhere to pile porcelain. Moreover, the two gangs in Huizhou, who used to hold the financial hub, have exhausted their finances due to the bandit washing in the previous year and cannot release any funds. The porcelain merchants who used to serve as money lenders and pawnshops cannot turn around now and can only sit and wait for death. At present, except for a few who have strong capital and are still starting work, 80% to 90% are in a state of suspended animation. Various factories, households, and kiln owners cannot maintain it and are willing to pay severance fees and dismiss workers. Therefore, the number of unemployed workers is increasing day by day, and it is desolate. If this continues, I am afraid that in a few years, the Jingdezhen porcelain industry will completely collapse. (November 12th)

Jiangsu Provincial Construction Conference Concludes 70

▲ Transportation Organization Plan Approved

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department convened the heads of construction bureaus and offices from various counties to hold a conference in the province, which lasted for six days. It passed a total of more than 100 proposals from six groups: water conservancy, municipal administration, electricity, administration, finance, and transportation. Today (20th) at 10:00 a.m., a closing ceremony was held in the auditorium of the Construction Department, where Director Dong Xiujia delivered a speech, encouraging the heads of various bureaus and offices not to do nothing because of lack of funds, but to strive to invigorate themselves, exhaust their efforts, and work hard to carry out construction work. Then the meeting was adjourned.

The transportation group's proposals were discussed on the 19th evening. Because most of them were in line with the decisions of the Seven Provinces Highway Conference, they were successfully passed. However, the construction of a light railway from Guazhou to Qingjiang was reserved for the time being due to various difficulties. As for other proposals, (1) completed highways are to be opened to merchants to operate automobiles, (2) a car factory is to be set up, (3) labor is to be conscripted annually for road construction, (4) ship registration is to be carried out, (5) consolidation of Daoqing is to be encouraged (that is, using earth pits to solve agricultural water conservancy disputes), (6) effective maintenance and conservation methods for completed roads, bridges, culverts, telephones, and other projects are to be stipulated, all were amended and passed, and the department will formulate methods for implementation. (20th)

Local Correspondence

Kunshan 71

▲ Female Prisoners from the Third Branch Prison Sent to Kunshan for Temporary Custody The Jiangsu Third Branch Prison and the High Court Detention Center were crowded with prisoners, so they negotiated with the Kunshan Detention Center for temporary custody. Yesterday at noon, Director Zhao Zhen of the prison and detention center, together with the guards, escorted 20 female prisoners from Suzhou to Kunshan. After inspection by Director Miao, who also served as the director of the detention center, they were clearly received and imprisoned.

▲ County Farmers Association Appeals for Poor Farmers Poor farmers in this county often pawned their rice during the autumn harvest when rice prices were low. The local Farmers Bank in this county had set up one or two storage and pawnshops in the past two years. The procedures were cumbersome, the interest was high, and the facilities were not widespread, making it difficult to popularize. Xu Xusheng, the executive director of the County Farmers Association, was aware of this and specially requested the county government to consult with the Provincial Farmers Bank to order the Kunshan branch to provide loans to various district offices, which would act as storage and pawnshops. The facilities would be widespread and the interest would be lower, so that farmers could benefit.

Jiangyin 72

▲ Supervisory Committee Sends Letter to County to Seal Up Opium Company The County Party Department Supervisory Committee held a meeting yesterday (18th) because the so-called Chengxing Company in this county was openly selling opium, which was a clear violation of the Prime Minister's will. It was decided that (1) the county government should be instructed to seal up the company as soon as possible, (2) a report should be submitted to the Provincial Supervisory Committee, and (3) a public letter should be issued to the masses to unanimously reject drugs. On the same night, an official letter was sent to Wang, the secretary acting as the county magistrate, hoping to receive a reply on the handling of the sealing up.

▲ Military Police Special Service Team Seizes Bandit Communist A week ago, six military police officers, including military police officer Yuan Zhong, deserted from the Boke team of the 3rd Regiment of the Capital Military Police. The headquarters immediately ordered the search for them. A few days ago, Wu Jianqiu, a member of the Special Service Police Team, seized Yuan Zhong, a box gun, and more than 50 rounds of ammunition in Room 2 of the Wai Jiaotong Hotel in Chengbei. On the 18th, he was sent to the Public Security Bureau for detention. On the 19th, he and team member Gu Wenyi ping escorted Yuan Zhong to Wuxi for interrogation.

Nantong 73

▲ Provincial Security Corps Executes Notorious Bandit in Tong The Provincial Security Corps stationed in Tong County arrested a notorious bandit, Wang Fugen, in the northern township. After confessing without denial, Zhu, the head of the regiment, submitted a report to the Security Office, which approved the execution of the notorious bandit at the Yaolu intersection in the city on the evening of the 19th.

▲ Allotment and Distribution of Land Tax in Tong County The Finance Department has allocated the number of land tax allotments and distributions in Tong County, estimating that the annual quota is more than 88,000 yuan. After deducting various items for local expenditure, which amount to more than 35,000 yuan annually, there is still more than 52,000 yuan remaining. The average monthly payment should be more than 4,400 yuan.

▲ Fourth Prison Implements Expansion The Jiangsu Fourth Prison has been ordered by the Ministry of Judicial Administration to expand and include the three counties of Rugao, Haimen, and Qidong as branch prisons. Sun Xiong, the warden, has already made preparations, and fundraising for expansion expenses is also underway.

Wuxi 74

▲ Lü A'gen Sentenced to Death for Premeditated Murder A certain son of Cheng Genfa, a resident of Fenlongqiao Township near Houqiao in the 9th district of the county, joined the Communist Party in the 17th year of the Republic of China. Later, he suddenly regretted it and did not associate with ordinary party members. The party members were afraid that he would leak secrets and be detrimental to the party, so Lü A'gen recruited Cheng's son to go out to eat mutton soup, killed him, dismembered him into six pieces, and abandoned him in Yuanshan Pond. Later, the county government arrested Lü and transferred him to the court to file a public prosecution. Yesterday at 2:00 p.m., Lü A'gen was sentenced to death for the crime of premeditated murder and sentenced to one year of imprisonment for the crime of damaging the corpse. He should be executed. After hearing the verdict, Lü A'gen declared in court that he was dissatisfied and prepared to appeal.

▲ Villagers March in Teams to Protest Taxes Chen Henian, director of the Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Bureau in this county, counted that there were more than 1,000 households in the urban and rural areas producing and selling liquor. The total amount of liquor produced annually reached about 30,000 dan. The public sale tax was more than 20,000 yuan annually, and the most was in Xin'an Township. In July last year, the former Wuxi Yin Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Bureau submitted a report to the general bureau for approval to collect taxes in accordance with the regulations. However, Tuo Zhimo Yongsen and others in Xin'an Township recently gathered crowds to march in teams, distributing anti-tax slogans and forcibly resisting. However, according to Article of the Provisional Regulations on Tobacco and Alcohol Business License Tax, Item 2, the business situation of each liquor-producing and selling household should be taxed in accordance with the regulations and grades. The households that have already paid taxes have all started to follow suit, and other merchants have also expressed their intention to be treated the same. The general bureau director has been requested to issue a document to the county government of this county to earnestly inform the merchants to cooperate in the collection of taxes. After receiving the report, Director Jiang specially instructed County Magistrate Chen to inform the merchants and people to pay taxes in accordance with the regulations and not to resist on the pretext of violation.

Changshu 75

▲A rice boat was robbed in Wangjingtang. Shi Jinsheng, a boatman from Xiaodongmenwai Xiaohetou, loaded fifty shi of white rice the day before yesterday to be shipped to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, at about 4 a.m., when passing through Wangjingtang, two grain boats suddenly approached and blocked the way. Seven or eight strong men jumped onto the boat to search and rob, resulting in the theft of more than ten dan of white rice and over eighty silver dollars.

Yangzhou 76

▲Water and land military police jointly suppressed bandits. Hu Weiyun, head of the third district security corps, and Tao Hongru, head of the three hundred, reported that bandits were entrenched in Xinzhengxing Town. A detective team was dispatched in disguise to investigate. It was found that bandit leader Liu Shoubiao led more than one hundred bandits with over forty guns and a dozen Mauser pistols. They were a combined gang from Haizhou and Shouzhou, residing in the beach during the day and going to town to smoke and gamble at night without any scruples. Police chief Wei Tinghui was sent to the Fifth District of the Water Public Security Bureau to consult with Director Zhao, who approved the dispatch of the Daya warship for joint suppression. At the same time, the Third Battalion Commander of the stationed Yangzhou regiment under the county was dispatched to assist. On the 18th, at night, Captain Wei and Battalion Commander Yang led their teams to the destination and, together with the warship, simultaneously ordered an encirclement and suppression, arresting bandit leader Liu Shou. Abducted victims were rescued, and the search is ongoing.

Gaoyou 77

▲Bandits threatened extortion and set fire to a house after failing. Zhou Fangshi, a farmer from Baima Temple in the county, has already been robbed twice this year. The day before yesterday, he received another threatening letter from bandits, demanding five thousand yuan. Because Zhou found it difficult to raise such a large sum, he moved to the city temporarily to take refuge. The bandits came to the village the night before last to collect the money and, seeing that the gate was locked, became very angry. They set fire to Zhou's straw storage room, burning more than two hundred dan of rice. They threatened that if Zhou Fangshi did not hand over the money, they would come back and set fire to the entire village.

▲An elderly woman was kidnapped and escaped back late at night. The aunt of Zhu Mingwen, a villager from Nanzhuzhuang in the third district of the county, who is over eighty years old, was kidnapped by bandits at the beginning of the month. Her eyes were covered with plaster, and she was hidden in a nearby grassy marsh. The woman took advantage of the bandits' sound sleep the night before last to escape on her own. It was indeed fortunate.

Educational News Highlights

Ministry of Education Announces High School and Junior High School Curriculum Standards 78

The Ministry of Education has announced the curriculum standards for primary schools and kindergartens, with the exception of civic training. The high school and junior high school curricula are being announced in succession, including high school history, music, English, biology, physical education, arithmetic, Chinese culture, and chemistry; junior high school chemistry, music, English, arithmetic, Chinese, hygiene, history, physical education, manual arts, botany, and zoology. High school also includes ethics, geography, drawing, civics, and physics; junior high school also includes home economics, geography, drawing, and civics, and other subjects whose courses are being revised and will be announced in succession soon. The Ministry of Education also recently announced the total weekly teaching hours for each subject in high school and junior high school, as well as the total weekly hours for extracurricular sports and self-study at school.

Ministry of Education Promulgates Kindergarten and Primary School Curriculum Standards (4) 81

II. General Outline of Primary School Curriculum Standards

First, the Overall Goals of Primary School Education

Primary schools should develop children's physical and mental health, cultivate the basic knowledge and skills necessary for national morality and life, and foster citizens who know etiquette, righteousness, love the country, and love the community, based on the Three Principles of the People and in accordance with the educational purpose and implementation guidelines of the Republic of China. The analysis is as follows:

(1) Cultivate children's healthy physique.

(2) Nurture children's good character.

(3) Develop children's aesthetic interests.

(4) Enhance children's knowledge and abilities for life.

(5) Train children's habits of labor.

(6) Inspire children's scientific thinking.

(7) Cultivate children's spirit of mutual assistance and unity.

(8) Foster children's concepts of loving the country and the community.

Second, Scope of Work 1. Subjects and Total Weekly Teaching Time Table

Upper Grades 60 60 80 390 180 150 210 150 90 90 1560 Middle Grades (Third Grade, Fourth Grade) 60 60 150 390 120 120 180 240 120 90 90 1380 1440 Lower Grades (First Grade, Second Grade) 60 60 150 390 90 90 60 150 90 90 90 1170 1260 (Grade Minutes Subject) Civics Training Hygiene Physical Education Chinese Language Social Studies Nature Arithmetic Manual Arts Fine Arts Music Total Remarks The above scores can all be divided by three, making it easy to distribute as one side with thirty, forty-five, or sixty minutes.

(Explanation) 1. Civics training is different from other subjects and focuses on individual training in normal times. The time listed in the table is for group training time. 2. Each subject may be divided or combined according to the specific local situation. The methods are as follows: (A) Social studies, nature, and hygiene can be combined into one subject of general knowledge in primary schools. (B) The manual arts and agricultural arts operations can be set up as a single type, namely, naming it as a certain subject, such as the one set up. Other necessary operations are incorporated into the respective subjects with similar properties | for example, a special art subject, with agricultural gardening and housework incorporated into the nature subject (C) The fine arts and manual arts subjects can be combined into a work subject in the lower grades. 3. Three time periods is a moderate number and can be increased or decreased by ninety minutes per week depending on the local situation. 4. Time allocation is based on thirty minutes per section and is extended to forty-five or sixty minutes depending on the nature of the subject material.

II. Weekly Time Score Table for Other Group Activities

Grade Minutes Remarks

Lower Grades 180

Middle Grades 270

Upper Grades 360

Morning Assembly, Weekly Meeting, Commemoration Week, Extracurricular Sports, Extracurricular Homework, Children's Autonomous Group Activities, etc. Group operations are all included. (Explanation) 1. The time for various activities may be determined according to the local situation. 2. Activities are set up according to the scope and nature of each school.

Third General Education Principles

(1) When arranging the weekly homework schedule, attention should be paid to the nature of each subject, striving for a balance between difficulty and ease, physical and mental balance, appropriate time length, and even distribution per week... Special attention should be paid to facilitating contact, ease of teaching.

(2) The selection of teaching materials for each subject should be based on the goals of each subject, with the most important principles being suitability to the current and local needs of society and the experience of children.

(3) The guidance of civics training is not in the teaching of texts and theoretical exploration, but should guide children to practice in the areas of school, family, and social life.

(4) Textual teaching materials should be described in vernacular Chinese and should not use classical Chinese.

(5) The organization of teaching materials should strive to link each subject to form a large unit, so as to reduce the disadvantages of fragmentation, mixing, and repetition.

(6) Before teaching, teachers should have sufficient preparation, not only to fully understand the teaching materials used, but also to prepare a teaching plan (at least a brief lesson plan), appropriate teaching aids, and the teaching environment should also be made as good as possible.

(7) Teaching should focus on "doing", should adapt to the psychology of children, arouse children's reactions, indicate the purpose of the activities to be achieved, arouse children's interest, concentrate children's attention, and guide them to develop activities, conduct their own experiments, and make efforts to proceed, so that children "use both hands and brains", "practice what they preach" to "do" it, this is the only and most important principle of teaching.

(8) All parts of the teaching materials that require children to practice repeatedly (such as the recognition and memory of words, the proficiency of writing, the familiarity of place names, personal names, and dates, the familiarity of arithmetic, the familiarity of songs, etc.) should use the method of "practice teaching", and the conditions that must be taken into account are as follows: 1. The materials should be taken from children who already understand the meaning, 2. The time should be short and the number of times should be many (for example, writing, practice once every day or every two days, each time no more than fifteen minutes), 3. The method should adopt proven experimental methods and should be more varied (several methods should also be used for practice in one short time), 4. Success is only achieved when the predetermined standard is reached, 5. Attention should be paid to the results, first seeking accuracy and then speed.

(9) All parts of the teaching materials that require children to think precisely (such as the problems discovered in each subject, the causes and effects of historical facts, the doubts discovered in daily life...) should use the method of "thinking teaching", and the conditions that must be taken into account are as follows: 1. The following steps should be used frequently to assist children: (A) Action, (B) Discovering difficulties, (C) Determining the location of difficulties, (D) Various methods of solving difficulties, (E) Selecting the most effective method for experimentation, (F) After repeated trials and experiments, make a judgment, 1. Teachers should not be impatient, should not act on their behalf, and should not be arbitrary. Children should be allowed to think calmly. 3. Should earnestly guide children on how to act, how to collect materials, and how to organize materials. 4. Develop children's attitude and habits of respecting objective facts and not adhering to their own opinions.

(10) All parts of the teaching materials that require children to appreciate (such as stories, poems, songs, works of art, natural scenery, etc.) should use the method of "appreciative teaching", and the conditions that must be taken into account are as follows: 1. It is best to let children choose their own materials, 2. It is appropriate to arouse them by implying tones and attitudes, 3. Use methods such as description and comparison to supplement children's imagination and guide children's appreciation, 4. Within the possible scope, it is appropriate to guide children to compare and study various points such as beauty and ugliness to enhance children's ability to appreciate, but it should still be based on arousing children's emotional response as a principle, and it is not appropriate to have children excessively analyze and criticize, so as to lose the purpose of appreciative teaching, 5. The individual differences of children should be clearly understood, and it is not appropriate to hope that everyone will get the same results.

(11) All parts of the teaching materials that require children to express themselves (such as the performance of stories, the production of handicrafts, the creation of articles, the production of pictures...) should use the method of expressive teaching, and the conditions that must be taken into account are as follows: 1. It is necessary to predict whether children can do it successfully, and choose to do what they can do, 2. Choose materials that are easy to get results and easy to achieve the purpose, 3. Have a desired goal and a detailed plan, 4. During the production, teachers should try to encourage children and help children as appropriate so that children can succeed and be satisfied 5. No matter the success or failure, be sure to follow the plan and make results.

(12) Teachers should pay close attention to the achievements of children, and the examination of achievements and the standards of achievement should take scientific methods.

(13) Teachers should clearly identify the children's physical condition, personality, family, environment, etc., observe them meticulously, record them carefully, prescribe the right medicine, formulate a unique educational plan, implement teaching carefully, and strictly examine the results, not only for the increase of knowledge and skills, but also for the cultivation of all good habits of civic training and the elimination of bad habits.

(14) Teaching is not limited to subjects and schools. In addition to subjects, what else to teach and how to use outside the classroom and school, etc. should be studied and implemented at all times. (To be continued)

Ministry of Education Explains Methods for Repairing Confucius Temples 82

The Ministry of Education, based on the Jiangsu Department of Education's inquiry about the methods for repairing Confucius Temples, specially instructed an explanation, saying that the buildings of Confucius Temples should be repaired by the educational administrative organs that manage the Confucius Temples, and the repair costs should be included in the annual budget. If they cannot be borne independently or if the Confucius Temple has no property, they should consult with the county government to jointly discuss repairs with local organs.

The Ministry of Education believes that the submitted documents are quite useful. ▲Walking for twelve hours... advancing in three routes

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Boy Scout Regiment, for the purpose of practicing outdoor life and paying respects to the Songhu war zone, specially dispatched the third-term members of the regiment yesterday to the war zone for a twelve-hour walking trip. They were divided into two routes for advancement. ▲ Escape from Death. The singles final began at 1:30. Yu Tianguang served first and attacked first, but lost the first two games, then lost by one to three. He fought hard to make it three to three, and then three to four, finally making it four to four. Yu served hard, regaining one game, and thus escaped from death at five to four. He initially showed his talent and won the first set with a score of six to four.

▲ Utter Defeat. In the second set, Yu's strokes touched the net every time, and he achieved very little. His opponent Burrenzhi attacked fiercely and won three games in a row, then became five to one. Yu was utterly defeated and although he won back the first game, he lost two to six.

▲ Reclaim Priority. Starting from the third set, Yu played cautiously, and both forehand and backhand strokes were extremely strong. Burrenzhi also did not show weakness, and the two sides fought fiercely. Initially, the situation was even, but after three to three, Yu finished it in one go, and regained priority with six to three.

▲ Constant Grievances. In the next set, Yu's momentum became even stronger, with powerful serves and sharp strokes, determined to win the victory. He once occupied an absolute advantage with a four to one lead. However, in the following few games, Yu's serve was repeatedly judged as a "foot fault" by the referee, and Yu became timid and lost his control, allowing Burrenzhi to take the opportunity to attack and reverse the situation to win seven to five. Yu's defeat was a pity. If Yu's serve was a foot fault, then Burrenzhi's "walking serve" was even more of a foot fault, but the referee did not penalize it even once, so everyone cried injustice for Yu Tianguang.

▲ Persist. Yu Tianguang trembled and tried his best to cheer up. In the fifth set, Yu had priority every time. Although Burrenzhi tried hard to follow and did not show any weakness, he finally became flustered and lost points frequently after four to four, losing two games in a row, and Yu won with six to four. Yu thus won the championship with three to two.

5 | 7

Lin Baohua 6 | 2 Burrenzhi

Mrs. Medimo 7 | 5 Mrs. Dufozhi

Following the previous group was the mixed doubles final. Lin Baohua and Mrs. Medimo faced Burrenzhi, who had failed in the singles final, and Mrs. Dufozhi, the grass court tennis singles champion. Lin Baohua fought hard and did not disappoint his hard work, which was a pleasant surprise.

▲ Lost the First Set First. The battle began, Burrenzhi served first, and always took the lead, occupying the advantage in one game, which was evened out by the Lin Baohua group. Lin's group's victory can be said to be entirely due to Lin alone. Mrs. Mei rarely made contributions, while the opponents were quite evenly matched. After five to five games, Bur and Du added two games in a row, winning seven to five.

▲ Reclaim Rights. Heaven's Gift, Luck Should Win. On the second set, Mrs. Mei suddenly gained energy, and her strokes were powerful and deep to the baseline. Lin Baohua's strength was added, and he was even more determined to fight and won four games in a row, which was very easy. As a result, Lin and Mei won six to two in this set, reclaiming the rights.

▲ A Bundle of Blessings. The third set was the key to victory or defeat. Both sides played carefully and did not show any weakness, but at the beginning, Mrs. Mei showed signs of weakness again, and made mistakes one after another. Lin Baohua stood alone, and had the regret of neglecting one thing and losing another, which led to the loss of one game in a row, which was terrifying. Unexpectedly, the opposite came, and Mrs. Mei, who was plump, was blessed by the stars, and suddenly changed her weak state, cheered up, and made contributions again and again. Lin got her help and won four games in a row, and took the lead with four to three. However, in the following two games, each lost one, and Lin and Mei still ranked last with four to five. The next game was Mrs. Mei's serve, and the audience was worried for her, thinking that her weak serve would be more dangerous than auspicious, and knew that she had won the game, safely survived the crisis. Then the hope of the Lin group came, when Burrenzhi served, Lin Baohua fought hard to win back, and the next game was Lin Baohua's serve, and he easily scored the last victory with seven to five. Although it is said that it was Lin's effort that led to this, Mrs. Mei's blessing cannot be denied. Although her technique was mediocre, she was able to control it calmly at a critical moment yesterday, which was the main reason for the victory.

New Basketball Techniques ㈢㈡ (Not to Be Reprinted) Original by Clare Burcky, Jointly Translated by Zhang Guoxun and Qian Yiqin 101

This strategy is not the usual action after the center jump, but the person who receives the ball from the center has the responsibility of blocking the opponent's center, which can give the team a lot of benefits, because it can make the team's center, unexpectedly, penetrate deep into the opponent's area and attack unprepared.

Center #3 jumps up and hits the ball to #2. Before #2 receives the ball, he passes it to #1, who cuts diagonally across the court. Then #2 immediately blocks the opponent's center from advancing, allowing the team's center #3 to sprint down the right sideline to receive #1's pass, then dribble forward a few steps and throw it in from under the basket.

Local News

Today's League of Nations Meeting: Expression of Chinese Public Opinion; He Minhun and Others Plead for Restraining Japanese Aggression; National Salvation Association Sends Telegram Requesting Rejection of Joint Administration Proposal 102

▲ Letter from He Minhun and Others to the League of Nations Assembly Addressed to Messrs. Yan, Gu, and Guo, the Three Chinese Delegates to the League of Nations in Geneva, to be Forwarded to the League of Nations Assembly.

Gentlemen,

The primary mission of this assembly is to seek a peaceful resolution to the Sino-Japanese issue. This is something that the Chinese people find gratifying, and we should express our respect to you. However, it is reported that your assembly will seek a solution to the problem based on the so-called report of the investigation team. On this point, we, He Minhun and others, must solemnly inform you of the views of the Chinese people.

The Manchurian issue is, in fact, the focal point of the Sino-Japanese issue. From its own perspective, it undoubtedly possesses its own complex international character. However, the process by which the Manchurian issue arose and its subsequent escalation were clearly caused by Japan's historically rooted imperialist aggression against China. The frenzy of the Japanese militarists, the manifestation of their aggressive policies, and the erroneous views of Japanese capitalists all sought to take advantage of the unprecedented global panic to monopolize Chinese Manchuria and Mongolia in order to alleviate their own panic. Consequently, they used the "Nakamura" incident as a pretext to forcibly occupy Chinese Manchuria and Mongolia, falsely claiming to the world that they were defending against Russia in an attempt to deceive the world and create immense chaos and disputes, threatening humanity with the brutality of war.

Since the sudden outbreak of the Mukden Incident on September 18th of last year, Japanese imperialism has disregarded the condemnation of the world and used force to seize our Northeast Three Provinces. Prosperous Manchuria has been reduced to a desolate wasteland by Japanese artillery fire. The chaos and terror have not only caused widespread disturbance, but they have also created a puppet organization mixed with Japanese ruffians, plunging the lives of thirty million compatriots in the Northeast into the most cruel and displaced conditions of human existence. The loss of life and property, though still lacking precise statistics, is estimated to be in the tens of millions.

In this situation, the League of Nations' Executive Council failed to fulfill its due responsibilities, and the international covenant upon which the League of Nations is founded was completely shattered by the artillery and machine guns of Japanese imperialism. As a result, the military actions of Japanese imperialism have become even more frantic and increasingly pressing. On January 28th of this year, they even attacked Shanghai, reducing the most important Jing'an and Wusong areas, the crystallization of national culture and industry, to scorched earth. The loss of life and property of our compatriots in Shanghai is incalculable.

It is suspected that the intention of Japanese imperialism is nothing more than to divert the attention of the world from the Manchurian issue and to suppress the resolute resistance of our compatriots nationwide to the Japanese invasion of the Northeast. However, the Executive Council failed to impose sanctions on Japan from the outset, effectively allowing the situation to escalate. This is deeply regretted by the Chinese people.

The Executive Council considered its best effort to resolve the Sino-Japanese issue to be the dispatch of an investigation team. We do not wish to overly criticize the team itself. Although we, the Chinese people, never had any expectations for the team's visit, we still hoped that the team could provide a concrete and substantial explanation of the content and process of the incident, so that the world could understand the truth of the matter. However, the report submitted to your assembly after the team's six months of investigation and research is merely a display of devious and skillful writing. It not only fundamentally lacks an accurate understanding of the truth and development of the incident but also clearly exhibits a pro-Japanese bias and a major international conspiracy. In essence, it transforms Japan's exclusive occupation of the Northeast Three Provinces into international joint administration, openly implementing the partitioning of China, completely ignoring the rights and demands of the Chinese people. This is resolutely opposed by the Chinese people, leaving no room for tolerance. This must be brought to the serious attention of the assembly.

The Manchurian issue itself is the key to world peace. This is obvious and need not be elaborated upon. Japanese imperialism's armed occupation of Manchuria is a direct attack on the Chinese people and, indirectly, a challenge to the world. It has not only provoked widespread resistance to Japanese imperialism's aggression among the Chinese people and created a confrontational situation between China and Japan but also triggered a global upsurge in anti-imperialist aggression among oppressed nations, putting the entire world on a war footing.

Here, the thirty million people of our Northeast, in a world where so-called justice and righteousness are insufficient to rely on, must turn to self-reliance and launch a heroic struggle against the aggression of Japanese imperialism. The "Manchukuo," manufactured by Japanese imperialism, is openly falsely presented as the will of the so-called "Manchurian residents." This kind of blatant distortion of facts further demonstrates its shameful tyranny and barbarism.

The conspiracy of Japanese imperialism is not only to plunder Manchuria and make it its exclusive colony but also to seize Jehol as a base for attacking North China and disrupting all of China, thereby triggering a global war. A few months ago, Japanese imperialism appointed its ruffian Ishimoto Ken'ichiro as a senior staff officer of the Kwantung Army and ordered him to go to Jehol to collude with Chinese traitors and realize its grand scheme to seize Jehol. Regarding this conspiracy and its important and compelling evidence, our army intercepted Ishimoto and seized numerous secret documents. This compelling evidence can be made public to the world at any time. Japanese imperialism, realizing that its conspiracy had been exposed, instead used the Ishimoto incident as a pretext to launch an armed invasion of Jehol, constantly bombing with artillery and airplanes, intending to turn the area between Chaoyang and Nanling into ashes. All the atrocities witnessed in Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Shanghai are being repeated in Jehol. All of this could have been personally heard and seen by the members of the investigation team at the time. How can it be denied?

Now, as you convene in Geneva to discuss the Sino-Japanese issue, Japan is once again actively attacking Jehol, launching fierce attacks on the front lines of our army on the Jehol border, forcing our six million compatriots in Jehol, under the threat of violence, to unite with the thirty million compatriots in Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang to more resolutely expand the anti-Japanese struggle. As a result, the situation in Jehol is becoming increasingly serious and deteriorating. Jehol is currently a crucial key to war and peace in the future of the Sino-Japanese issue, as well as a crucial key to the future of the Far East. This must also be brought to your serious attention.

You must understand that the current resolute attitude and demands of the Chinese people are entirely due to the violent oppression inflicted upon us by Japan. We have thus gained a deeper understanding. We firmly believe that the liberation of the Chinese nation can only rely on its own efforts. Only the power of our truly mobilized people can shoulder this great mission. However, if you unfortunately disregard our demands, we vow to use our heads and iron blood to exchange for the true independence and freedom of the Chinese nation. The Chinese people's opposition to the aggression of Japanese imperialism is a war of self-defense and will surely receive the assistance of the people of the world and gain the trust of all oppressed nations. This must also be brought to your serious attention.

What must be further stated here is that our resistance to Japan is only a resistance to the imperialist aggression that Japan has inflicted upon us. We have no hatred or malice towards the Japanese people. Our army is a popular armed force in Jehol resisting Japan, and it is one of the armed groups representing the thirty-six million Chinese people in Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Jehol. We are determined to coexist with the territorial sovereignty of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Jehol, and we will not hesitate to make any major sacrifices to strive for the integrity of our territorial sovereignty. Here, we do not hesitate to present the following main points to you:

㈠ The Chinese people resolutely oppose any solution to the Manchurian issue based on the principles and recommendations of the investigation team's report, and resolutely oppose imperialist aggression and the partitioning of Chinese territory.

㈡ The demand of the Chinese people is the true independence, freedom, and liberation of the Chinese nation.

㈢ Until the territorial sovereignty of Manchuria is fully recovered, the Chinese people's war of resistance against Japan will not end.

Gentlemen of the assembly, if you can thoroughly recognize where the key to peace and war lies, you should fundamentally stop Japan from abandoning its imperialist aggression, unconditionally return the Northeast Three Provinces to the Chinese people, immediately withdraw its troops stationed in China, and abandon all rights acquired through imperialist aggression. If you follow Japan's demands and continue to delay and evade this issue, this is absolutely not what we expect from you.

Respectfully submitted by He Minhun, Chairman of the Military Committee of the National Anti-Japanese Army of Jehol, China; Zhang Zizhao, Vice Chairman; and members Liu Liquan, Li Ciru, Xia Naitang, Wang Shuren, Wu Leiyuan, Yang Zhen, et al.
