Japan's Opinion on the Report 103

Our Diplomatic Circles... Believe It Has No Value for Comment

▲ Equivalent to Denying All Sino-Japanese Agreements

▲ And Not Recognizing Its Diplomats in China

The New Voice News Agency stated that the contents of the Japanese government's absurd opinions on the Lytton Report, transmitted by the Japanese News Agency, are generally considered by diplomatic circles in this port to have no value for comment. However, it is believed that one matter is worth mentioning, namely, that when Acting Executive Yuan President Soong Zi-wen refuted the remarks made by a certain responsible Japanese official, "I do not know where the actual government of China is, who is in charge," he said, "Japanese Minister Arima Akira has just presented his credentials to the National Government a few weeks ago. If the words of the Japanese official are true, it is equivalent to not recognizing his own minister." In Japan's opinion on the Lytton Report, such absurd statements are recorded. This is actually equivalent to a written statement that Japan does not recognize all its diplomatic officials stationed in China, that is, it formally denies the validity of all international agreements between China and Japan. At the same time, it can further confirm the statement of American politician Peck that "When any country signs an international treaty with Japan, it must sign one copy with the Japanese Foreign Province and one copy with its General Staff Headquarters." Not only that, but even the diplomats Japan sends to foreign countries must be recognized by its General Staff Headquarters before they can be official.

China's First Female Aviator, Ms. Lin Pengxia, Goes to the Northwest for Inspection 104

Huang Jingwan Hosts Farewell at Moore Memorial Church

Female aviator Lin Pengxia, from Fujian, has traveled to various European and American countries to study aviation, politics, and economics and has gained considerable experience. She is one of the earliest Chinese women to study aviation. After graduating, she followed her father in business in Singapore, but this was not her original intention. Since the September 18th Incident in the Northeast, she has planned to return to China alone to join the volunteer army and work on the front lines, but she was unable to do so for other reasons. When the Shanghai Battle broke out, she resolutely set out and came to Shanghai by ship, but the government had already signed a peace treaty, and the war had ended, while the Northeast Incident had not yet been resolved. Many patriotic youths in Shanghai have organized rescue teams to go north, but the importance of the Northwest is no less than that of the Eastern Provinces, and the Xikang disputes in recent years have been extremely serious, but Chinese people have generally turned a blind eye to it. Ms. Lin has the determination to go to the Northwest alone for inspection and will depart north tomorrow. Yesterday afternoon, Mr. Huang Jingwan specially hosted a banquet at the Moore Memorial Church on Third Road to bid farewell and invited many enthusiastic people in aviation and national salvation to accompany her. Lin Pengxia, Wang Shuzhen, Su Zuqi, and three ladies, and Huang Jingwan, Wu Mai, Yin Zhiling, Tan Bozhi, Xu Beihong, Xu Tongye, Huang Miao, Cao Zhongyuan, and other thirty people attended. During the banquet, Huang Jingwan and Wu Mai gave speeches. Next, Ms. Lin described the purpose of this trip, saying in essence that the importance of the Northwest is even greater than that of the Northeast because the Northeast has always had the support of the Han people, so after it was lost, the people still felt it and issued a painful cry. The Northwest, however, has undeveloped culture and superficial public wisdom. Once an accident occurs, there is no way to recover it. This trip is to investigate the political and economic situation in the Northwest and to find ways to develop it. Many of the people present are enthusiastic about border affairs, and I hope they will pay attention to it. Next, Mr. Shi Dianfeng from Qinghai gave a speech, saying that the land in the Northwest is extremely vast. Taking Qinghai Province as an example, it is about seven times larger than Jiangsu, but the population is sparse, and the financial resources are abundant, but no one is developing it. Xinjiang and Tibet have even larger areas, few Han people, complex customs, and mountains everywhere. They do not interact with the people of Central Plains. They have long wanted to form a Great Tibet country. All the records of the locals say how China is and how the Tibet country is, as if Tibet has been separated from Chinese copyright. Moreover, the Turkish leader once advocated the idea of ​​a Great Northwest country, which would unite Turkey, Afghanistan, Xinjiang, Tibet, and Qinghai into a Great Northwest country. The plan has been long planned and is in active progress. Because Chinese people do not pay attention to the Northwest, the actual situation is extremely dangerous. If the Northeast is lost, there is still the volunteer army making a final struggle. The people of the Northwest have absolutely no awareness. This time, Ms. Lin's trip to the Northwest should use the culture of the Southeast to guide the compatriots in the Northwest. Next, Mr. Huang Heqing gave a speech, saying that when he was studying aviation in the United States, he visited a certain place in Hudson Bay where the products and books of the Northwest were displayed. The Americans praised the Northwest as the paradise of the world and said that the Ottawa Conference should be held in the Northwest. Foreign countries pay so much attention to the Northwest of China, but we do not pay attention to it. How can this be? Ms. Lin has the determination to develop the Northwest. We should congratulate her on her success. Tan Bozhi and Yin Zhiling gave speeches on the importance of aviation and national salvation, hoping that Ms. Lin will promote aviation in the various places she passes through, so that the inland people will also have the opportunity to save the country. Mr. Cao Zhongyuan reported on the Northwest inspection by the Science Society for Ms. Lin to use as a reference. Finally, Mr. Yang talked about his experience of serving in the Northwest for more than ten years, saying that the people of the Northwest are all simple, honest, and kind and express extreme friendliness to people from the South.

Chinese Tram Workers Refuse to Resume Work Yesterday Despite Order 105

▲ Union Directors Claim Persuasion Ineffective

▲ Company Decides to Follow the Proclamation

After the Chinese Tramway Company workers went on strike, the Municipal Government and Municipal Party Headquarters jointly issued a proclamation, limiting the resumption of work by yesterday noon. At that time, all the workers resisted the order. The company is preparing to hire new workers to find ways to restore the operation of electricity. The government has decided to punish the workers who resist the order and strictly arrest the leaders. The details are as follows.

▲ Strike Situation After the full strike of the workers in the Transportation Department, the Chinese tramways on lines 1, 2, 3, and 4 continued to be suspended yesterday. However, the French trams, lines 3 passing through the Chinese territory, Xiaodongmen to Ximen, line 5, the railway station to Ximen, and line 6, the 16th Wharf to Lujiawan, all passed through Ximen as usual. In the company at Chezhan Road, only the director of the Transportation Department, Lu Zhonglin, and the staff and workers were left. The fourth squadron of the Police Brigade sent four teams of armed policemen to be stationed there. The waterworks in Gaochang Temple were guarded by soldiers of the security team, and the security was very strict.

▲ Refusal to Resume Work The Municipal Government and Municipal Party Headquarters jointly issued a proclamation limiting all workers to restore to their original state before 12:00 yesterday morning. Yesterday morning, Lu Zhonglin, the director of the Transportation Department of the company, prepared everything according to the manager's order, waiting for the workers to enter the factory and resume work. By 1:00 pm, the workers still had not resumed work. The manager was immediately reported on the situation and reported to the Party and government agencies for verification.

▲ Union Persuasion A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited yesterday.

Page 10

Fu Chongde and Hu Yida, executive directors of the First District Water and Electricity Workers Union, claimed that after the Party and government agencies issued a proclamation limiting the resumption of work, the directors and supervisors of this union went to advise the workers to obey the order and resume work on time. However, all the workers believed that the company had no sincerity in the salary increase issue. Now, (1) the salary increase issue must be resolved, and (2) injured workers must have a corresponding solution before they will resume work. The union was unable to force them because the workers' will was like this, so it had to wait for legal action. However, it hoped that the company would make concessions and contact the union. Now, the person in charge of the company is away, and the union has no way to contact him.

▲ Bureau Chief Inspects At 11:00 yesterday morning, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, Wen Hongen, led inspectors to the Chinese Electric Company on Chezhan Road for inspection. Seeing that all the workers violated the government orders and refused to enter the factory to resume work, he instructed the police officers stationed there to strictly guard against them and immediately returned to the bureau. Although the Social Bureau, the Municipal Party Headquarters, and the Public Security Bureau were closed yesterday as usual on Sunday, in the case of the Chinese Electric Company strike, in addition to the personnel on duty, senior officials were also assigned to stay behind.

▲ Determined to Punish Strictly The reporter from the New Voice News Agency learned from the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Public Security Bureau, the Social Bureau, and other agencies yesterday that the workers who violated the orders of the Party and government agencies and refused to resume work would be dealt with according to the handling steps decided by the Municipal Government and the Municipal Party Headquarters the day before. The company was allowed to dismiss the workers who refused to resume work, and at the same time, new workers were recruited to actively restore the operation of the trams on each route to maintain transportation. The Public Security Bureau will strictly arrest the leaders of the strike and investigate them according to law. The union, which had failed to provide proper guidance, will also be severely punished.

▲ The Company Expresses A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited the executive director of the Chinese Electric Company yesterday. He said that the company has always treated its workers very well. The average wage is about 30 yuan. Workers with longer seniority and diligent work can receive an additional 136 yuan in wage increases and awards each year. In addition to their monthly wages, they also receive 3.5 days' wages, which are saved and accrue interest in accordance with the 5-year life savings plan, and are paid out after the 5-year term. If they are sick, there are Chinese medicine and designated hospitals to provide medical care and medicine, and wages are still paid. According to the law, those who die on duty have funeral and pension expenses of 350 yuan, plus two years of average wages. In this company, regardless of whether they die on duty or not, they are bound by previous contracts and are paid in full. Often, one worker dies and thousands of dollars are paid. Those with higher wages receive even more than this number. There are also festival rewards for the annual holidays. Such treatment is probably rare in factories across the country. Since 1928, regardless of diligence, good or bad work, seniority, or depth, all have been given a universal increase of 2 yuan in accordance with the agreement. The agreement expired at the end of June this year. The company submitted a request to abolish the universal wage increase on schedule, believing that it was an evil system in theory and in fact. The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau issued a standard for handling labor-capital disputes the year before last, which also stated that the universal increase system should be abolished because it is an unfavorable measure for both industry and commerce and the workers themselves. At the same time, the company formulated a salary table for workers of all levels and methods for promotion and salary increases to show fairness. Unexpectedly, the union proposed a divided salary increase and other conditions, glorifying it as a demand for equal treatment for employees. How can equal treatment for employees be defined? It cannot be solved in a few words. Moreover, this year is a time of national crisis, and there is also a world economic panic, and the company's business is mediocre, and the cost of living is low. If this can be increased, when will it not be possible to increase? All the reasons why wages cannot be increased will be announced when necessary. However, the workers dared to violate the Party and government agencies' order prohibiting strikes, ignoring everything and suddenly striking in the midst of a mediation that was proceeding in accordance with the law, thinking to hide it by stealing the car keys. However, they did not know that the more they tried to cover it up, the more obvious it became, and it showed that their minds were exhausted. For the time being, let us not discuss where the keys were hidden. Why did the workers say that even if they had the keys after the company issued the spare keys, they would not drive the car today unless they were allowed to increase their wages? It can be seen that this is a very clear organized strike. In recent years, the workers of this company have been extremely arrogant, and they have often gathered crowds to coerce and besiege them. The company has always been magnanimous and accommodating, and has accommodated everything that can be negotiated, hoping for labor-capital cooperation. Who knew that the labor side would make progress and repeatedly pick up trivial matters, relying on the crowd to show off their strength and infringe on the company's right to employ people and drive them away. Last time, in the matter of Zhu Shaoyi, the director of the Transportation Department, Executive Directors Wang Yiting, Gu Xinyi, and Zhang Xiaoliang came to the company to persuade them, but they were besieged by the workers for six hours, and even made rude remarks and refused to listen to persuasion. Recently, because they obeyed the order not to give holidays and double pay on National Day, the workers actually despised the government orders and resented Feng Liutang, the secretary-general of this association, and beat him severely, causing him serious injuries. He has not been able to work until now. In addition to besieging the manager this time, they also destroyed the doors and windows of the manager's office and reception room. This company is a public utility, which is related to local security and the lives of citizens. The actions of these workers should have been rectified long ago, but in this state of violent kidnapping, once rectified, there will inevitably be many problems. I am afraid that the outside world will not be aware of it and will be confused by the malicious words, and all the hard work that the company has put in over the years will be in vain. I had to be patient until now, not daring to intentionally ignore it. Fortunately, the Party and government agencies have clearly investigated the facts and handled them according to law. The company has a glimmer of hope, but since the Party and government agencies announced to the workers that they would resume work at 12:00 am today (20th), this company immediately sent supervisors to prepare for the workers to come to the factory to resume work. However, no one reported to work until the afternoon. The workers' disregard for the Party and government agencies, their violation of government orders, and their arrogant attitude can be seen from this. This company has only to follow the measures in the proclamation "If you dare to disobey, you will be allowed to dismiss the investors and recruit new workers," and has already submitted a written report to the Party and government agencies for record, and will recruit new workers to restore the original state, in order to facilitate the public.

The Northeast Recovery Association Yesterday Published an Open Letter to Overseas Chinese Compatriots 106

▲ Elaborating on the hardships of the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army in the Northeast

▲ Deeply Hope Overseas Chinese Compatriots Will Actively Donate Money

According to the Far East News Agency, Cheng Qian, Li Liejun, Bai Wenwei, Zhang Zhijiang, Fu Rulin, and other members of the Central Committee recently contacted overseas returnee compatriots and representatives of the Anti-Japanese armies stationed in Shanghai to organize the Northeast Recovery Association to provide substantive support to the Northeast Volunteer Army, with the aim of recovering the lost territory in the Northeast. The association yesterday specifically issued an open letter to overseas Chinese compatriots, elaborating on the brutality of the Japanese invaders and the arduous struggle of the Volunteer Army, hoping that the compatriots would actively donate money, concentrate their efforts, and save the country from peril. The original text reads: "To our overseas Chinese compatriots: The violent Japanese, relying on their military force, have occupied our Northeast for over a year. The lives and property of the people of the three provinces have been subjected to the slaughter, plunder, trampling, and humiliation by foreign invaders, beyond any calculation. The weak writhe in the arena of knives and saws, while the strong fight for their lives under the arrows. Wherever the iron cavalry arrives, villages and markets are reduced to ruins. Those captured are buried alive, the dead are dismembered, the cruel punishment is worse than torture, and the massacre extends to infants. The grievances of the dead fill the sky, and the remains line the roads. Such a tragic disaster is unprecedented in history. Our military and civilians in the Northeast are not only filled with the fear of national subjugation but also deeply feel the pain of personal experience. Since General Ma Zhanshan began the resistance last October, the self-defense forces and volunteer armies of various provinces have risen like the wind and surged like clouds, fighting bloody battles, advancing wave upon wave, to confront the violent Japanese and have persevered until today. The Japanese invaders have not been able to rest easy for a single day. The righteous cause has inspired the whole country and moved the world. The extension of the frontline in the Northeast has enabled the initial maintenance of the situation. However, the violent Japanese, gaining an inch, seek a mile, and become even more brutal. From occupying the Northeast, they proceeded to organize a puppet state, and recently even blatantly and brazenly recognized it. In terms of military affairs, within two months, they secretly deployed more than ten divisions of heavy troops to various parts of our Northeast, hoping to launch a large-scale offensive when the green gauze tents are removed, launching a three-pronged advance against our loyal and valiant Volunteer Army under Tang Juwu, as a large-scale general attack. This is their vicious plan, which has already begun to be implemented. If the Volunteer Army perishes, then the Northeast will perish with it. If the Northeast perishes, then the areas of Pingjin and Rehe will also perish along with it. Even if our national people do not want to be slaves of the Japanese invaders, how can they possibly achieve it? This is truly a critical moment of survival, and it is what our national compatriots should act upon swiftly and devote all their efforts to. Since the fall of Liaoning and Panjin, the people of the whole country have been heartbroken and shedding tears, all thinking of risking their lives to fight the Japanese invaders. It was only because the government tolerated and conceded, always relying on the League of Nations, believing that justice could provide protection. Now, the report of the investigation team has been published. The so-called advisory conference, Manchurian autonomy, Sino-Japanese new treaty, etc., spare no effort to destroy our country's territorial sovereignty, while expanding the economic rights and interests, consular jurisdiction, residence, and land lease rights of Japan to an unlimited extent. In summary, it is nothing more than using our country's territory for the control of the great powers, and giving the greatest real power and important interests to Japan, who first initiated the incident. This kind of booty-sharing proposal even wants our country's government to make an official declaration, to acknowledge it on their own initiative, and to be responsible for prohibiting 'resistance goods' as a condition for obtaining it. This is not only to seize our Northeast as being sufficient, but also to cut off and suppress the vitality of its recovery. The unreliability of the League of Nations has already been clearly revealed. We have no other hope but to use iron and blood as weapons for self-salvation and self-defense. This is especially what our national people should be clearly aware of and urgently rise up to plan for. Recently, national elders, overseas returnee compatriots, and representatives of the Northeast Volunteer Army have gathered in Shanghai, all considering that the situation is urgent, the enemy is deep, and the danger to the Volunteer Army is imminent. It is appropriate for each to do their best and quickly plan for rescue and support. Therefore, the Northeast Recovery Association was established, proclaiming its purpose and methods as follows: 1. This association is jointly initiated by domestic people, overseas compatriots, and representatives of the Northeast Volunteer Army, focusing on raising funds to support the Northeast Volunteer Army for continued and sustained struggle. In particular, it aims to unite overseas compatriots and the Northeast Volunteer Army, concentrate national talent and strength, form a united group, and mobilize together as the basis for recovering lost territory. 2. This association establishes a board of directors to preside over internal affairs. It temporarily establishes three groups: economic, military, and political, to assume various responsibilities. It hopes that overseas compatriots and the Northeast Volunteer Army will send more representatives to participate in the association's affairs, in order to jointly plan progress and strive for expansion. 3. This association takes a national stand, recognizing that supporting the Northeast Volunteer Army is equivalent to national self-support. Therefore, regardless of party affiliation or gender, anyone who agrees with the association's proposals can join the association in accordance with the articles of association, with the aim of awakening the national people to jointly shoulder the responsibility of saving the country. 4. The association's economic matters advocate absolute transparency, and are handled by the economic group. Domestically respected elders, overseas returned overseas Chinese, and representatives of the Northeast Volunteer Army are publicly elected, each in a certain number, to serve as economic committee members, presiding over the raising of funds and the disbursement and distribution of affairs, ensuring that the supporters and the supported directly participate and jointly shoulder the economic tasks, in order to demonstrate great credibility and increase practical effectiveness. 5. The Volunteer Army supported by the association must be those currently fighting on the front lines and have been confirmed by investigation. This investigation task is the responsibility of the military group. 6. The funds raised by the association are designated to be collected by the bank (the name of the bank will be notified separately by letter). The above-mentioned points should be followed by colleagues and will not change from beginning to end. The troops inside the passes are all subject to restrictions, and at a time of shared hatred of the enemy, it is necessary to support the anti-Japanese volunteer army in carrying out its obligations in order to achieve the goal of recovering the lost territory. Recent arrivals from outside the passes all say that the Volunteer Army is hungry and has no food, cold and has no clothing, wounded and has no medicine, dead and has no burial. At night, they use grass as their bedding, and when exhausted, they lean against rocks to block the spears and bullets. When retreating, they are also met with the howls of tigers and the cries of monkeys. In the past, from the cold to the warmth, they could barely support themselves. Now, the severe cold outside the passes, with the solid ice submerging their shins, and the Volunteer Army with their bodies of flesh and blood enter and exit from among airplanes and artillery, and must struggle against the frost and snow. This is the first urgent need for assistance. What we hope for from the Volunteer Army is not that they can immediately recover the lost territory, but that they can continue to carry out a sustained resistance. Therefore, battle may not necessarily be won immediately, but it is not permissible not to fight. Attack may not necessarily be successful, but it is not permissible not to attack. Defense may not necessarily be solid, but it is not permissible not to defend. The reason why the violent Japanese do not hesitate to spend huge military expenses and do not hesitate to destroy public justice and international treaties, and must brazenly seize our Northeast, is to seize its rich resources, internally to increase the prosperity of their country, and externally to use it as a base for conquering China and invading the world. After occupying Liaoning and Jilin, they are eager to complete the Jihui Railway, expand the scope of the South Manchurian Railway, and implement immigration and reclamation and other economic constructions. And the task of our Volunteer Army is to destroy their various completed and soon-to-be-completed constructions, and hinder their current and to-be-implemented plans. Although they occupy our land, they will never be able to use the land. Although they seize our industry, they will never obtain the benefits of the industry. If we persist in this for a long time, the violent Japanese, although strong, will inevitably undergo great changes internally. This is the second urgent need for assistance. National spirit is an element of modern nation-building, so the more dangerous the country becomes, the more the national spirit is encouraged, because its will cannot be taken away. Since the Northeast was handed over to the enemy, all nations have ridiculed us, mocking our nation as having no national concept or ability to organize a country. The violent Japanese took this as an excuse to seize it, and the investigation team regarded it as the root of humiliation. There is no greater shame than this. Fortunately, the comrades of the Volunteer Army have risen up on the frontiers, vowing to fight to the death. National glory and national personality rely on this to regain a little. Judging from past battle achievements, the more powerful forces, such as Ma Zhanshan and Li Qinghai in Longjiang, Li Du, Ding Chao, Feng Zhanhai, Gong Changhai, etc. in Jilin and Heilongjiang, Wang Delin in eastern Jilin, Deng Tiemei and Tang Juwu in Liaodong, Zhu Jiqing in western Liaoning, and Geng Jizhou, Feng Guanxiong, Cheng Changkui, Zheng Guilin, Jin Ziming, etc., have all fought hundreds of battles, large and small, with outstanding achievements that are obvious to everyone. Even the other brigade regiments are all striving to be enterprising and generously serving their lives. Therefore, wherever the military forces point, the mad bandits are swept away. They entered Shenyang before and recovered Jilin Province later. Although they all withdrew due to insufficient weapons and ammunition, their loyal and courageous spirit is enough to reach the clouds and chill the enemy's courage. Recently, Su Bingwen, Zhang Xiangge, and other brigades of more than 20,000 people have once again rebelled and united in various parts of Manzhouli, driving directly to the Black Border. Taking into account the three provinces, the Volunteer Army with systems and organization has no less than 400,000 people, destroying their homes to relieve the country's difficulties and sacrificing their lives to save the country. Everyone shares the same heart. If our national compatriots can take advantage of the situation to rise up and provide assistance, filling their military strength, providing them with weapons and ammunition, and providing them with clothing, food, and supplies, it will not be long before all the compatriots in the Northeast become volunteer soldiers, and the return of our land is not far away. This is the third urgent need for assistance.

The compatriots outside the passes are stretching their necks and looking forward, their eyes full of blood and tears, looking forward to our national people for a long time. For the past year, people at home have been running around shouting and advocating for donations and assistance, and have also exhausted considerable efforts. And our overseas Chinese compatriots, gathering large sums of money, have been remitting them continuously, which is especially enthusiastic and touching. However, because the Volunteer Army is located on the border, the passes and rivers are far away, and they are restricted and imprisoned, and the overseas compatriots are ten thousand miles away, separated by the ocean, and it is even more difficult to connect with them. Therefore, even though assistance is provided, the needs of the military are urgent. It can be seen that this matter is of great importance, and it is difficult to achieve success without relying on the wisdom and efforts of the masses. And the people at home, the overseas Chinese compatriots, and the Northeast Volunteer Army, are especially unlikely to achieve full effectiveness unless they are united and concentrate their entire strength. This is what the members of this association should strive to implement day and night. Overseas Chinese compatriots are devoted to the motherland, as is known to all colleagues. In the creation and maintenance of the Republic of China, they often save on food and clothing and enthusiastically donate money, becoming the pioneers of the people at home. Now, at the beginning of the organization of the association, we hereby state the outline to inform you, hoping you will carefully consider it. Initiated by the Northeast Recovery Association, standing directors Cheng Qian, Li Liejun, Bai Wenwei, Zhang Zhijiang, Fu Rulin.

The Volunteer Army Support Association Assists the Volunteer Army in Northern Manchuria 108

▲ The Variety Show Was a Great Success

The Shanghai Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, in view of the tense situation in Northern Manchuria, believes that if assistance is not provided continuously, there will be no way to supply food and boost morale. Therefore, it decided yesterday to allocate 40,000 yuan to provide assistance. As for how this money will be distributed, it will be discussed at tomorrow's regular meeting, so that it can be remitted immediately, and a telegram will be sent requesting continued efforts in the anti-Japanese work and perseverance to the end.

The variety show held by the association last night at 7:00 PM at the Tianchan Stage was attended by upper-class people. The front of the stage was crowded with cars and horses, and the tickets for the flower balconies and boxes were completely sold out. Although there were a few who purchased the tickets but did not go to the show, the seats were still filled with people, showing that people sympathize with the aid to the Volunteer Army. And all the amateur performers and artists also showed their skills, performing vividly and colorfully, truly extraordinary. Even today's variety show tickets were purchased from the association yesterday in an endless stream.

Five of the Seven Robbers Are Fugitives from Taicang Prison 111

▲ Committed Six Robberies in Shanghai

▲ Several Robbers Admitted, Several Robbers Prevaricated

The bandits Sheng Yunsheng, Zheng Shanghe, Zou Zhongxi, Chen Chunhe, Li Guodong, Gao Yunshan, and Xu Shouzheng, between March and October of this year, formed a gang and held weapons to rob Chen Anquan at No. 54 Dongxi Huaide Road, Chen Wangshi at No. 103 Xinji Bang Road, Xu Xinfu at No. 87 Baker Road, Liu Laowu at No. 31 North Chengdu Road, Wang Weiwen at No. 350 Tangjia Lane, and Yin Yangshi at No. 273 Donghan Bili Road, etc., for property worth more than 1,500 yuan, and fled. After the case was exposed, they were successively arrested by Chinese and Western detectives of the Huishan Patrol Room, and a pistol and five bullets were seized. They were escorted to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. Yesterday, Judge Zhao Linyu came to the Third Criminal Court to interrogate the defendants separately. Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer of the patrol room, stated, "Please expedite the conclusion of this case, as the defendants, except for Zou Zhongxi and Chen Chunhe, are all escaped prisoners sentenced by the Taicang District Court. They will be transferred." When questioned, Sheng Yunsheng admitted to robbing North Chengdu Road once, Zheng Shanghe admitted to North Chengdu Road, Tangjia Lane, and Donghan Bili Road three times, Zou Zhongxi admitted to Tangjia Lane once, Chen Chunhe completely denied it, Li Guodong claimed to have been a special agent in a certain army, but had already resigned and came to Shanghai to look for friends but failed to meet them and was detained while staying at the Aido Hotel, and overturned his previous confession to the patrol room regarding the Dongxi Huaide Road case, Gao Yunshan and Xu Shouzheng both denied robbing and made evasive statements. The patrol room lawyer Zhang detailed the confessions of Chen, Li, Gao, and Xu, who were pointed out by Sheng Yunsheng and Zheng Shanghe as accomplices in robbing Chengdu Road, Dongxi Huaide Road, and Baker Road. Judge Zhao declared to the four defendants, Chen, etc., "How can you exonerate yourselves by prevaricating in court?" He then appointed lawyers to defend each defendant pro bono and ordered them to be remanded in custody pending sentencing. It was found that the crimes committed by the defendants in Taicang who had been sentenced were Sheng Yunsheng and Zheng Shanghe (both robbery), Li Guodong and Gao Yunshan (both cigarette workers), and Xu Shouzheng (kidnapping). All five criminals escaped from prison on March 3 of this year.

Criminals Also Have Good and Bad Luck in Committing Crimes 112

▲ Committed the Crime Before March 5

▲ Invited to Reduce and Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

▲ Otherwise, They Should Be Executed by Firing Squad

Wang Xunfu from Yangzhou, on the evening of January 10 of this year, at about 11 o'clock, along with Jiang Dinghui and others who have been sentenced to death and executed, robbed the property worth more than 270 yuan at the home of Wang Yu, a widow from Shaoxing, at No. 71 Taian Lane, North Shanxi Road, and kidnapped her to extort a large sum of money. After the case was exposed, he was found by Chinese Detective Shen Chongli of the Hongkou Patrol Room and escorted to the First Special District Court for interrogation and trial. Yesterday, Judge Shen Bingrong came to the Third Criminal Court and sentenced Wang Xunfu to life imprisonment for the crime of jointly kidnapping for ransom, and sentenced him to four years and eight months of imprisonment for the crime of jointly robbery, to be executed as life imprisonment, and declared to him that the case occurred before March 5, otherwise he would be executed by firing squad.

Water Disaster Relief Committee Invites Representatives from All Sectors to Inspect and Repair Dike Works in Various Regions 113

▲ Departing from Shanghai on the 26th of This Month

The National Government's Water Disaster Relief Committee, in order to inspect the dikes along the Yangtze, Huai, Han, and Yun rivers and water diversion projects repaired with work relief funds, hosted a banquet yesterday noon at the Bank Club for representatives from various sectors. Those in attendance included Simpson, F.W.S. Oehme, Wen Lanting, Lin Kanghou, Liu Zhanen, Zhang Shouyong, Zou Bingwen, Zhao Jinqing, Li Zhaohuan, Pan Xulun, Yu Xiji, Tai Xieqing, Wu Zhihao, Wang Zhixin, (Xu Peihuang as representative for) Wu Tiecheng, Chen Liting, Liu Yunfang, as well as the Committee's Secretary-General Zeng Rongfu, Committee members Li Zushen, Huang Renlin, and over fifty others. Committee Chairman Song Ziwen was absent due to other engagements. The banquet was presided over by Vice-Chairman Sir Simpson, who delivered a speech, followed by Secretary-General Zeng Rongfu, who reported on the progress of dike repairs and the significance of inviting representatives from all sectors for inspection. Next, the Director of the Committee's Engineering Department, Xi Mingjiu, reported on the itinerary for inspecting the various engineering sections and immediately sought out attendees willing to conduct the inspection. Those who signed up at the time included Zhang Shouyong, Liu Zhanen, Li Zhaohuan, Lin Kanghou, Wen Lanting, Chen Liting, Yu Xiji, Wu Zelin, Wu Zhihao, and the foreigner F.W.S. Oehme, totaling over ten people. The event concluded at 2:00 PM. Regarding the inspection of dike projects, the Committee has appointed Huang Renlin as the chief host, with Zeng Rongfu also serving as the Deputy Director of the Preparations Office, responsible for internal matters, to ensure swift progress. A separate record of Mr. Li's report and the scheduled inspection itinerary is provided below.

▲ Mr. Li's Report Mr. Li Zushen reported, in brief, that last year's devastating floods prompted the Committee to implement work relief measures in addition to providing emergency relief, with the aim of addressing the fundamental problem. The decision was made to repair various dike sections and water diversion projects using work relief methods. While the floodwaters were still receding, the Vice-Chairman, accompanied by water conservancy engineering experts, conducted aerial surveys of water levels and topography. Once the floodwaters had receded, the Engineering Department, in conjunction with the provincial Construction Bureaus and Water Conservancy Bureaus, commenced construction, which took a year to complete. The required funding was largely provided by generous donations from various sectors in Shanghai. Their deep concern for the people's livelihoods and their emphasis on water conservancy are deeply appreciated. With the completion of the dike works, representatives from all sectors are respectfully invited to inspect the results, demonstrating that the donated funds have not been wasted and to seek guidance, ensuring further improvements, ultimately achieving lasting benefits and preventing future flooding.

▲ Invitation for Inspection The original letter from the Committee inviting representatives from all sectors to inspect the works reads: "Respectfully informing you, the floods last year caused immense devastation. In addition to providing emergency relief, this Committee, adhering to the principle of 'work for relief,' has repaired the main dikes along the Yangtze, Huai, Han, and Yun rivers, as well as the water diversion projects in the lower reaches of the Huai River, all of which have been completed one after another. Since the establishment of this Committee, we have deeply appreciated the enthusiastic support from society and the generous donations, for which we express our profound gratitude. This Committee has scheduled a trip on November 26th, renting a China Merchants Steam Navigation Company vessel, to depart from Shanghai and conduct an inspection along the works. We have long admired your concern for water disasters and your emphasis on dikes and dams. Therefore, we have sent this special invitation, hoping you will condescend to join us and personally inspect the works. Your invaluable guidance and supervision will benefit the thousands of miles of dikes. We would be extremely fortunate. Enclosed is a schedule of the inspection project dates. We respectfully request your review. If you are willing to accept this invitation, please respond within two days, and we will send you a boarding pass. We will wholeheartedly await your arrival."

▲ Scheduled Itinerary The Committee's scheduled itinerary for inspecting the engineering projects in various regions includes the following: The Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei major dike project, from November 26th to December 2nd, departing from Shanghai and inspecting in sequence: (First District) the dikes at Foganzhou, Guadong Shuangzha, Hekou, Tongjing, etc.; (Second District) the dikes at Siheshans, Wuhu, Lugang, Huangsitan, Daijia, Longtan Dam, Gengtou, Liubai zhang, etc.; (Third District) the Yangtze dikes in the Datong area, Saozhougou, Zongyang, (Majiawo) Guangrenwei, (Dadukou) dikes; (Fourth District) the dikes at Laozhoutou, Chenjiaying, Duanyao, Xiaochikou, Guanhu Port, Xujiawan, Zhujiacun, Wuxue, Ganjiang Yichengwei, Qingfengwei; (Fifth District) the Fankou Dike, Maoshan Dike, Baishazhou, Wujin Dike, Wufeng Dike, Wuhui Dike, Zhanggong Dike, Hankou Flood Control Dike. From December 3rd to December 6th, proceeding upstream along the Yangtze River from Hankou to inspect: (Sixth District) the Jinkou Dike, the dikes near the New Dike; (Seventh District) the dikes near Jianli, the Zhu San Gong Dike, December 7th to December 8th; (Eighth District) the Hanchuan Dike; (Ninth District) the Fangjiawan, Yangjiayue Dikes. Returning from Yuekou to Hankou. The Henan-Anhui border area, the lower Huai River, the Yi-Luo-Huai-Yun projects, from December 9th to December 12th, again departing from Hankou to Zhengzhou to inspect in sequence: (Tenth District) the Shahe, Yinghe projects, and the Yi-Luo River project. From December 13th to December 17th: (Twelfth District) the Huaiyuan, Luohe Street river dikes, and culvert projects; the Fengtai upper and lower Huai River dikes and drainage canal projects; (Eleventh District) the Youfei River mouth dike, the dikes near Zhengyangguan and Yinghekou; (Twelfth District) the Bei Fei River dike and dredging project, the Linhuai Guan Huai River dike; (Thirteenth District) the dikes on both sides of the Huai River from Wuhe to Fushan, and the Hui River Tuo River dike projects. From December 18th to December 20th: (Fourteenth District) the Shaobo, Gaoyou, Jieshou, west side of the Grand Canal earthwork, and the repair of breaches from Huaiyin Siyang to the Shandong border. From December 21st to December 24th: (Sixteenth District) the Minbian River, Xinyang Port, shortening and straightening the Caiwan, and dredging projects; (Seventeenth District) the Wanggang, Zhugang, Doulonggang, He Diao River shortening and straightening, and dredging projects; and the Sheyang River dredging project.

Northeast Refugee Relief Association Sends Out Donation Boxes 115

The Shanghai Charity Organizations' Joint Relief Association for Refugees, realizing that raising funds for the refugees has become increasingly difficult due to the ongoing national crisis, has resorted to broader appeals in hopes of accumulating small contributions. Yesterday, they sent out donation boxes to various public places, along with a letter stating: "Respectfully informing you, our compatriots in the Northeast have long suffered from the ravages of war and now face devastating floods. The dire situation is beyond words. We have established this association to raise funds for relief efforts. However, the disaster area is vast and the number of refugees is immense. It is difficult to provide comprehensive assistance without raising substantial funds. In addition to individual appeals, we have specially made donation boxes to be placed in busy locations, allowing kind-hearted individuals to make voluntary contributions. We hope that your esteemed organization (institution) (company) (hospital) will kindly display the box in a prominent location, making it easy for people to donate without coercion. When the donation box is full, please notify this association by telephone, and we will send someone to jointly unseal and count the contents, issuing a receipt. We kindly request your attention to this matter, as it concerns a benevolent act of disaster relief. Please take prompt action and reply to this letter. Furthermore, the Association received a reply from the New Pharmaceutical Industry Association yesterday, stating that, in response to the request to encourage members to donate a percentage of their sales for relief, the Association had previously received a letter from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, including measures for Shanghai industries to donate to the Northeast refugee relief effort. The Association had already resolved in a meeting to adopt the monthly donation method for six months. Although the fundraising channels are different, the relief destinations are the same. We inform you of this specifically for your information."

Li Guojie's Tuberculosis Returns While in Custody 116

▲ His Family Hires Jiang Yiping and Li Shirui for Legal Support

▲ Court Approves Bail Yesterday, but Release Delayed Due to Weekend

Li Guojie, the former general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was placed under surveillance after allegedly authorizing the unauthorized leasing of four godowns to the American China Trading Company. He was transferred to the District Court the day before yesterday. Now, Li Guojie is seriously ill, and his family has hired lawyers to seek bail for medical treatment. The details are as follows:

▲ Condition Worsens After being transferred from the Public Security Bureau to the District Court, Chief Prosecutor Xie Lian conducted two court hearings, charging him with dereliction of duty and malfeasance. He was ordered to be remanded to the court detention center. However, due to Mr. Li's weak constitution and advanced age of 51, he suffered from tuberculosis. The old ailment has recurred after being placed under surveillance. He has been coughing frequently since the night before, and although he has been treated by a court physician, there has been no improvement.

▲ Bail Approved After Mr. Li Guojie was detained, his family hired lawyers Jiang Yiping and Li Shirui as his representatives, requesting legal support. A reporter from "New Voice News" learned from lawyer Jiang yesterday that the court had approved bail pending further investigation, requiring him to be available for questioning at any time. Therefore, lawyer Jiang, along with Mr. Li's relatives, went to the District Court yesterday morning to request bail. However, as yesterday was Sunday, there were no responsible personnel at the court, so the effort was unsuccessful. It is now reported that bail will be posted today.

▲ Wife's Visit Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Mrs. Li, accompanied by relatives, visited him and brought clothing and other items. A reporter from "New Voice News" encountered Mrs. Li at the District Court and asked about Mr. Li's condition. She said that he was extremely heartbroken after being placed under surveillance and that his old illness had recurred and worsened. She specifically requested the President of the Court to approve bail so that he could be sent to a hospital for treatment. She came today to inquire about his condition but has not yet met with him. Since the matter is being handled by the judicial authorities, she will await a legal resolution.

Customs Notice Cancels Dalian Registered Private Vessels 117

The Customs authorities, because the Northeast Customs has implemented a blockade since September 25th, but Dalian merchants are still using registered private vessels to transport goods, specifically announced yesterday the cancellation, stating: "Regarding the announcement of matters, after closing the Harbin, Niuzhuang, Andong, and Longjingcun customs offices, and the measures for collecting taxes on goods traveling to and from the Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang provinces, and the methods for changing the treatment of private vessels traveling between domestic ports and Dalian or Niuzhuang Andong, have been issued in announcements No. 1241 and 1250. It has now been determined that the benefits of allowing private vessels registered for domestic port travel to trade with Dalian will be immediately canceled. Hereafter, private vessels wishing to trade with Dalian may only follow the Regulations for the Management of Maritime Private Vessels and Shipping by the Customs, and follow the regulations for overseas trade. Private vessels registered for domestic port travel will still be allowed to continue trading between Niuzhuang, Andong, and other domestic locations, but foreign goods transported from Niuzhuang and Andong may only be directly transported to domestic coastal areas with established customs offices, otherwise, the vessel and cargo will be confiscated. All private vessel shipping permits and registration books issued by the Niuzhuang and Andong customs offices after September 25th of this year will be invalid. All merchants should be aware of this notice."

Northeast Soybean Oil Taxation Issue 118

▲ Grain Association Urges Prompt Approval

The Shanghai Grain, Oil, and Cake Trade Association reports that soybean oil shipped from Yingkou, Andong, and other places in eastern Liaoning to Shanghai is now classified as foreign goods and taxed at several times the previous rate, creating an unbearable burden. The association has sent telegrams to the Ministry of Finance, requesting that it continue to be taxed as domestic goods, and has also sent representatives to Beijing, carrying a petition to the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance. However, no response has been received. Therefore, the association recently sent another telegram to the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, stating: "The case of soybean oil shipped from Yingkou and Andong to Shanghai, requesting that it continue to be taxed as domestic goods, has not yet been approved. The northern rivers are freezing soon, and the need for supplies in various places is critical. If a quick solution is not found, the supply will be interrupted during the three to four months of the freeze, and the people's livelihood will be severely affected, leading to panic. We urge you to approve the request as soon as possible." Shanghai Grain, Oil, and Cake Trade Association.

Committee Urging Dredging of Puhuitang River Visits Zhang and Hu 120

▲ Reported that Surveying of Songqing River Section Began Yesterday

▲ Requested Transfer of Consultation to Municipal Public Works Bureau for Assistance

The shallow and polluted Puhuitang River in western Shanghai is detrimental to the people's livelihood. Local gentry such as Ma Xiangbo organized a committee to urge dredging of the river and repeatedly requested the municipal government and the Songhu War Zone Rehabilitation Committee to allocate funds for dredging. The Rehabilitation Committee sent personnel to inspect the site and concluded that dredging was indeed necessary. They then submitted a report to the Executive Yuan and replied to the committee, requesting them to quickly prepare an estimate of the earthwork project so that funds could be allocated for construction, as previously reported. It is now learned that the committee has held a meeting and decided to invite specialized personnel to conduct surveying and prepare an estimate. As it is now winter, the appropriate time for dredging, the committee, eager to proceed, again dispatched representatives Yang Xinzheng, Chen Yafu, Li Youxian, and Gu Junjie to visit Zhang Shouyong and Hu Junzhuang, the executive member of the Rehabilitation Committee, to report that surveying of the Songqing River section has begun due to the harmonious cooperation between the governments of the two counties and the local gentry. They requested that the Municipal Public Works Bureau be consulted to assist in the Shanghai section, as the river is longer there, so that a complete estimate of the entire river can be prepared soon and bids can be invited for construction. They also stated that the Zaohua Bang River is polluted by sewage from the ditches on both sides, which flows into the river for dozens of miles, making the entire river black and smelly. Therefore, improving water conservancy requires the construction of a dam to intercept the flow to benefit the people's livelihood. Mr. Zhang also agreed that stopping the flow of foul water was indeed important, and that the construction of a dam and the diversion of the river had already been decided. "You are all enthusiastic about the local area, so please work hard and don't worry," he said. The representatives all said that they were grateful for the concern of Zhang and Hu for the people's suffering and expressed their gratitude on behalf of the people along the river.

Preparatory Committee of the Maritime Affairs Party Department Holds First Meeting 121

▲ Elected Yang Hu et al. as Standing Committee Members

▲ Passed Draft Organizational Rules

The Central News Agency reports on the inauguration of the preparatory committee of the Chinese Maritime Affairs Special Party Department, which was reported yesterday. The committee's office is still being furnished, and the temporary office is located at 18 Guoyutang Street in the South City. The committee held its first committee meeting immediately after the inauguration. The details of the meeting are as follows:

▲ Passed Resolutions The attending committee members were Yang Hu, Qian Yizhang, Yu Jiayong, Chen Su, and Wang Yongsheng. Yang Hu presided, and Shen Qiren recorded the minutes. (1) Passed the organizational rules of the committee. (2) Elected Yang Hu, Yu Jiayong, and Qian Yizhang as standing committee members. (3) The budget for regular expenses was resolved to be drafted by the standing committee members and submitted to the meeting for discussion. (4) Resolved to appoint Wang Yalen as the Director of the Organization Section, Liu Xigong as the Secretary acting as the Director of the Propaganda Section, and Liu Yulei, Liao Wenhua, Huang Shaoqiu, and Chen Jingzhao as secretaries. (5) Resolved that a regular meeting will be held every Thursday afternoon at 2:00 PM and a discussion meeting will be held every Monday morning at 10:00 AM.

▲ Inauguration Telegram To the Nanjing Chinese Kuomintang Central Executive Committee: "Hu et al. have been appointed by your committee as the preparatory committee members of the Chinese Maritime Affairs Special Party Department and respectfully took office at 10:00 AM this morning in the auditorium on the third floor of the Shanghai Municipal Party Department. At the same time, a swearing-in ceremony was held, and Committee Member Wu Tiecheng attended the ceremony to oversee the oath-taking. In addition to submitting a separate report on the inauguration, we hereby send a telegram for your approval." The Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Maritime Affairs Special Party Department, Yang Hu, Yu Jiayong, Wang Yongsheng, Chen Su, Qian Yizhang, [Seal].

▲ Organizational Rules Draft organizational rules of the preparatory committee of the Chinese Kuomintang Chinese Maritime Affairs Special Party Department: Article 1: These rules are formulated in accordance with the revised organizational regulations for the Maritime Affairs and Railway Special Party Departments. Article 2: This committee shall have three standing committee members, whose duties are as follows: 1. To convene meetings of the preparatory committee. 2. To review and issue documents of this committee. 3. To implement the resolutions of the preparatory committee. 4. To handle the external affairs of this committee. Article 3: This committee shall have one secretary, who shall handle daily affairs under the direction of the standing committee members, and supervise and evaluate the work of the staff. A Western-language secretary may also be appointed to handle all negotiations with foreign shipping companies and foreigners under the direction of the standing committee members. Article 4: This committee shall have four sections: General Affairs, Organization, Propaganda, and Labor Guidance, to handle all matters of their respective sections. Article 5: The duties of the Organization Section are as follows: 1. To plan the organization and training of lower-level party departments and the progress of training matters in accordance with the central organizational training laws and regulations. 2. To guide the lower-level party departments in their organizational and training work, and to evaluate their performance and correct their errors. 3. To handle disputes in lower-level party departments. 4. To participate in meetings of lower-level party departments and to supervise elections. 5. To handle the registration and review of party members' party membership. 6. To investigate the progress of party affairs and all temporary events. 7. To investigate reactionary elements. Article 6: The duties of the Propaganda Section are as follows: 1. To plan maritime propaganda work in accordance with the central propaganda plan. 2. To guide and evaluate the propaganda work of lower-level party departments. 3. To guide the organization and work of maritime cultural institutions, and to correct their errors and support their development. 4. To answer questions from lower-level party departments regarding propaganda. 5. To draft, edit, and review propaganda publications. 6. To distribute and print propaganda materials issued by the Central Committee. 7. To collect and review books that explain party principles. Article 7: The duties of the Labor Guidance Section are as follows: 1. To plan the organization of maritime labor organizations in accordance with the central mass movement laws and regulations. 2. To guide the organization and activities of maritime labor organizations and to correct their errors. 3. To guide and evaluate the work of lower-level party departments regarding the maritime labor movement. 4. To handle maritime worker training and education matters. 5. To handle labor and capital disputes involving maritime workers. 6. To investigate the distribution and living conditions of maritime workers. 7. To compile statistical reports and other matters. Article 8: The duties of the General Affairs Section are as follows: 1. To draft, receive, dispatch, store, and copy various documents. 2. To prepare agendas and records of committee meetings. 3. To prepare reports and statistics. 4. To supervise printing and proofreading. 5. To translate telegrams. 6. To handle accounting and general affairs. 7. Matters not belonging to other sections. Article 9: Each section shall have one director, who shall handle the affairs of his or her section under the direction of the standing committee members and the secretary. Article 10: Under each section director, there shall be several secretaries and clerks to assist, depending on the complexity of the section's work. However, the maximum number of staff shall be limited to sixty. If it is necessary to increase the number of staff due to special circumstances, the Central Committee must be notified for approval first. Article 11: The appointment and dismissal of the staff of this committee shall be decided by the committee. Article 12: This committee may establish a Finance Committee to manage party dues, budget estimates, final accounts, revenue and expenditure, and auditing matters. The organizational regulations shall be determined separately. Article 13: The detailed rules of procedure for this committee shall be determined separately. Article 14: These rules shall be implemented after being approved by the committee and submitted to the Central Committee for approval.

Coal and Stone Barge Industry Requests Relief for Inland Waterway Transportation 124

▲ Please forward to the Central Party Headquarters through the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

The Shanghai Coal and Stone Barge Industry Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating, "Respectfully, in the 14th resolution of the general meeting of your association on June 18th of this year, a request was submitted to the government to determine the ship registration authority to avoid double taxation. However, ships sailing in Zhejiang province still have to pay the ship license fee levied by the Zhejiang Provincial Government, amounting to a substantial four yuan and fifty cents to eight yuan per month, which are similar to miscellaneous taxes and should be abolished uniformly. Resolved, approved, and vigorously pursued. On June 26th of the same month, your association submitted a document to the Executive Yuan of the National Government, ordering investigation and prohibition to maintain the rule of law and avoid excessive taxation. On June 27th, a telegram was sent requesting the central government to delineate the scope of registration of the Maritime Affairs Bureau. However, five months have passed without approval. Moreover, at a time when commerce is declining and crises are looming, all ship merchants in the city are extremely apprehensive. If this continues, inland waterway transportation may even go bankrupt. Furthermore, we read in the newspaper on the 6th of this month that the Ministry of Communications, in response to the Shanghai Municipal Government's consultation on amending the organizational law of the Maritime Affairs Bureau to abolish the inland waterway registration office of the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau, replied to the Executive Yuan, stating, 'Received the Shanghai Municipal Government's consultation, according to

Page 12

the Public Works Bureau's reply, the Bureau of Maritime Affairs' ship registration is handled in accordance with the provisions of the Maritime Law, Ship Law, and Ship Registration Law, issuing nationality certificates to determine nationality and property rights, while the Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau registers ships to manage shipping administration within the Shanghai city area and maintain water public safety, which is the basis for collecting ship taxes. The authority and responsibility are clear.' In fact, the Maritime Law, as its name suggests, applies to ships sailing at sea, and nationality certificates were originally issued to manage foreign merchants. The registration of the Municipal Public Works Bureau is also handled in accordance with the Ship Law and Ship Registration Law. Now, the Maritime Affairs Bureau should not rely on the above two laws to re-register ships that have already been registered. Moreover, inland waterway merchants are all Chinese, and there is no need for proof of nationality. Even if proof of nationality is required, the ships already registered by the local government are sufficient to prove their nationality, without the need for double registration. The logic is also very clear. Moreover, inland waterway transportation relies on meager freight to maintain livelihoods. In recent years, taxes have become complex, and shipowners have been unable to cope. After registering and paying ship taxes with the Municipal Public Works Bureau, they must also pay ship license fees when traveling through Zhejiang province. Now, the authority of the Maritime Affairs Bureau has further encroached upon inland waterways, establishing registration offices in Minhang and Wusong, adding another layer of burden. Under these circumstances, the bankruptcy of the shipping industry is imminent. Therefore, we especially request your association to argue based on reason, submit a request to the Central Party Headquarters, and forward it to the Third Plenary Session to grant relief, and to promptly correct the registration issue for inland waterway vessels and the ship licenses in Zhejiang province according to law, to maintain commercial transportation."

Workers at the Fuli Rubber Factory Declared Resumption of Work Yesterday Morning 125

▲ Further submit to the Party and government for prompt mediation

All workers at the Da Zhongguo Fuli Rubber Factory on Xingjiazhai Road, Zhabei, demanded the restoration of their original wages, but to no avail. Instead, four representatives were dismissed by the management, leading to widespread indignation and a slowdown in work starting the day before yesterday. After officials from the Party and government were dispatched to persuade them, they resumed work yesterday morning. The labor side has submitted another request to the Municipal Party Committee and the Social Affairs Bureau for mediation, as detailed below.

▲ Resumption of Work Yesterday Morning After all workers at the factory declared a work slowdown, Zhao Zhenhua from the Municipal Party Committee and Chen Mingshan from the Social Affairs Bureau rushed to the factory at 3:00 PM the day before yesterday and earnestly persuaded the striking workers to resume work first and await resolution to avoid escalating the unrest. The workers expressed their acceptance but stated that it was too late to resume work that day, so all workers declared resumption of work yesterday morning.

▲ Labor's Submission After resuming work, the labor side submitted separate documents to the Municipal Party Committee and the Social Affairs Bureau, requesting prompt mediation. The original submission stated, "Respectfully submitted to ensure that all workers can work with peace of mind, requesting that the management be promptly ordered to provide a substantial response to the labor's demands to facilitate resolution of the dispute and protect workers' livelihoods. The workers, unable to withstand the oppression of the management, elected representatives and requested assistance from your departments. However, during the mediation period, the management forcibly pressured some workers to sign documents, causing panic among the workers who did not understand the truth, leading to the collective action of all workers leaving the factory on the 18th to petition your departments. All circumstances have been submitted by the representatives successively and reported verbally. It is found that the workers had no intention of slowing down work, but after the collective petition, they immediately returned to the factory to work. However, upon arriving near the factory, they suddenly saw a large contingent of police officers fully armed stationed inside and outside the factory. The factory manager, Yang Yongnian, and his wife also took separate cars to stop workers on the roads around the factory, causing the workers to fear entering the factory. On the 19th, after your departments dispatched personnel to investigate, they ordered the representatives to persuade all workers to enter the factory. Now, the workers have been persuaded by the representatives and have all entered the factory on the 20th. Based on the above facts, the responsibility for all disputes should be borne by the management. However, since the points raised by the workers have not been resolved and there is no definite response from the management as to whether they sincerely accept them, there is deep concern that the management may resort to other schemes. The workers are simple-minded and constantly apprehensive, so they instructed the representatives to submit another request to your departments to promptly order the management to begin negotiations to seek resolution and avoid other complications, and to protect workers' livelihoods. This is submitted with utmost urgency to the Shanghai Municipal Party Committee and the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau."

Maotai Co. Bombing Case Manager Wang Zhengtao Dies from Gunshot Wound 132

Maotai Foreign Goods Store at 310 and 312 Xinzha Road was visited by two male customers on the afternoon of the 18th, one wearing a long blue robe and the other wearing a long gray robe. Under the pretext of buying goods, each threw a bomb and opened fire, hitting the manager of the store, Wang Zhengtao, in the left waist. The bullet remained lodged in his abdomen and was sent to Baolong Hospital for treatment. This was previously reported in this newspaper. It has now been learned that after Wang was sent to Baolong Hospital, his fever increased, and the doctor deemed his condition untreatable. Although surgery was performed, the bullet could not be removed. He died at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday. It is reported that Wang was from Zhenjiang, and his wife and children are still in his hometown. The store has already telegraphed them.

Yesterday, the Hongkou Public Epidemic Hospital held a meeting to handle the closing. Assassination Case in Yanhai Road 134

▲ Four Suspects Arrested

On the evening of the 9th of this month, at around 7:00 PM, Zhang Zhigang (aka Zhang Asi) was shot and killed on Yanhai Road inside the Old North Gate, and the criminals escaped in the meantime. The Municipal Public Security Bureau received a tip that Zhang Xinsheng, who lives at 126 Fuyou Road and makes bone goods, and Jiang Asan, who lives at 157 on the same road, conspired to commit the murder. Director Wen immediately ordered officers from the Second Branch of the First District and the First Branch of the Second District to jointly arrest them. At 6:30 AM yesterday morning, Officer Hong Wensun and Wang Zhongqing of the First Branch of the Second District, under orders, led Sergeant Li Baoliang, Ma Yumin, Zhang Yichang, and Police Officers Wang Fengzhu and Zhou Ming, together with Police Officer Liu Chaoxiang of the Second Branch of the First District, secretly went to 126 Fuyou Road and arrested Zhang Xinsheng. They then went to 157 Fuyou Road and arrested four suspects, Ge Xingquan, Pan Jinsheng, Zhou Guirong, and Xu Weiquan. However, Jiang Asan was out at the time and escaped the arrest. They were all taken to the First Branch of the Second District for interrogation. According to the interrogation by Director Xu, Zhang Xinsheng and others confessed that Jiang Asan is a fellow trader whom they have known for more than ten years. When I got married yesterday, he came to give gifts and drink wine, but he did not live with me. He has no fixed place of residence and no fixed business. He usually lodges at the homes of various friends, especially at the home of Jiang Mingzhu in Beizhangjia Alley or at the Louis Industrial Factory on Singapore Road, etc. According to Ge Xingquan and others, the four of us work together and are in the bone goods business. We do not associate with Jiang Asan, but because of our business relationship, he did come to play and stay for one night three or four days ago, but we do not know the rest. As the case is related to conspiracy and the arrest was ordered, they were all sent to the Bureau for interrogation.

Handgun Found in Thatched Hut 135

▲ Five People Arrested and Sent to the Bureau

Lu Ying, the captain of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, in view of the upcoming winter defense period, supervised his subordinates to take turns going to the main passes in shifts from 3:00 AM to 9:00 PM every day to check pedestrians and vehicles. Particular attention was paid to all public places, hotels, teahouses, etc. The day before yesterday afternoon, Captain Lu received a report from Team Leaders Liu Shaoqing and Wu Xiufeng, who were sent to the Shanghai West Inspection Group, that they had joined the chief of the Sixth District General Office, police officers, and detectives from the Shanghai West Office of the team, Yu Maolong and Pei Yunzhang, and went to the Bailinan Road area to check pedestrians. When passing the intersection of Kaixuan Road, they suddenly heard the sound of playing with a handgun from a thatched hut at the corner of the road. Listening carefully, it seemed that several people were talking inside, and the situation was very suspicious. They immediately worked with the police officers to push the door open and saw five people in short clothes gathered around a table playing cards. They were about to go forward to check, but one of them immediately got up and ran away. They first grabbed the other four and bravely chased after the fleeing man, finally capturing him. They also found a six-inch Browning handgun with live ammunition and five bullets in the stove. They took them all to the team for interrogation. According to the confession of the suspect, Wang Hailin, the handgun and bullets that were found while I was making buttons were picked up when I was pulling a rickshaw during the Shanghai war and kept at home. This matter is known to Lu San. Now that the weather is getting colder and the clothes are thin, Lu San told me that someone wanted to buy it, so I took the gun to Lu San's house and showed the gun to Lu San in his room. I didn't expect that detectives would come in a short while, so I ran to the bed and pretended to sleep to avoid suspicion, and I was arrested. I did not intend to commit robbery. According to the confession of Zhang Xiaosan, I live in Lu San's house. Wang Hailin brought this gun, and after showing it to Lu San, he returned the gun to Wang Hailin. I went out to buy things, but unexpectedly detectives came in to arrest me. Wang saw that the situation was not good, so he threw the gun in front of the stove to escape. However, I don't know what Wang Hailin used the gun for. According to the confessions of Wu Lisheng and Shi Qing (aka Shi Zhuqing), we were passing by Lu San's door and went inside. We saw children holding playing cards and playing, and we didn't know anything else. Captain Lu believed that hiding firearms violated the law and ordered that the suspects, Wang Hailin and others, as well as the handgun and bullets, be sent to the Third Section of the General Bureau for legal action yesterday morning.

Meeting Record of Copyright Holders and Publishers 136

The Chinese Copyright Holders and Publishers Association was established in Peiping in July of this year. It was initiated by Hu Shi, Hong Xuefan, Zhou Zuoren, Xie Bingxin, Zhang Xichen, Shi Zuocai, and others. Its purpose is to connect sentiments, eliminate pirated books in North China. Since its establishment, it has achieved good results. Yesterday, the general secretary of the association, Shi Zuocai, came to Shanghai from Peiping. The association's Shanghai office specially convened a meeting of the publishing industry to welcome him. Representatives from more than 30 publishers attended, including Zhang Xishan from Kaiming Bookstore, Hong Xuefan from Modern Bookstore, Cao Zhusan from Beixin Bookstore, Shen Songquan from Guanghua Bookstore, Zhang Yiqu from Children's Bookstore, Tang Zhejuan from Huatong Bookstore, Zhou Wenqing from Shenzhou Guoguang Society, and Wang Meng from Yadong Bookstore. First, Chairman Hong Xuefan reported on the purpose of the meeting. Then, Shi Zuocai reported that the Shuangyi Bookstore and Qingyun Bookstore piracy cases recently uncovered in Peiping have been strictly investigated by the Public Security Bureau, and the association is proceeding with legal procedures to warn against cunning elements. This was passed by the assembly. It was also proposed that Bao Yulin, the director of the Peiping Municipal Public Security Bureau, should assist the association in cracking down on piracy. Unless he takes it seriously, east and west market book stalls have not dared to sell for half a year. Our copyright and publishing circles have benefited greatly. How should we express our thanks? It was resolved by the assembly that cultural institutions and various groups should formally express their thanks to show their appreciation of his virtuous policies. Finally, the chairman discussed the case of revoking Qingyun Bookstore's membership, the case of sealing up the Beixin Bookstore, the association's operating expenses case, the monthly dues payment case, the case of amending the association's charter, and the case of Sanyou Bookstore joining the membership. All were passed by a majority vote. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Anhui Compatriots Public Banquet for Anhui North Representatives 137

▲ Organizing a Support Association Against the North Salt Public Business Office

Yu Jihe and Lu Jianhou, representatives of the people from 21 counties in northern Anhui, came to Shanghai from Bengbu a few days ago to explain in detail the harm caused by the North Salt Public Business Office. The local Anhui Compatriot Association, according to the situation, sent telegrams to the National Government's Ministry of Finance, Salt Affairs Administration, Provincial Government, Commander-in-Chief Jiang, and Transportation Envoy Miao, requesting that the business office be abolished to benefit tax revenue and maintain people's food supply. Yesterday, the fellow villagers of the association held a public banquet for the two representatives. More than 30 people, including Shi Yinsheng, attended. Chang Fanhou was elected as chairman. Hong Zhenjiu gave a speech to express his condolences and the meaning of the banquet. Then, the two representatives reported on the progress of the case and the opposition of the people in Bengbu city and various counties, requesting the thorough support of overseas fellow villagers to achieve the goal of abolishing the office, relieving the people of their suffering, and expressing their gratitude. Ma Zhuqing, Liao Ziying, Li Pengfei, Jiang Zhifu, Wang Cibin, Zhang Liangfu, and others expressed their opinions, all of whom believed that the problem was very serious as it concerned the people's food supply and the future interests of merchants, and that an organization should be formed and listed as a special case to continue the struggle.
