Special reply, Anhui Provincial Government Cleverly Printed."

Provincial Order to Hold Native Cloth Exhibition 138

The Shanghai County Government yesterday received an instruction from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Industry, which said, "It has been found that the native cloth exhibitions held in Wujin, Shanghai, Nantong, and other counties this time have achieved remarkable results. Now that the national crisis has not ended and the people are competing for luxury, it is not enough to talk about saving the country without vigorously advocating thrift and enriching people's livelihoods. In order to promote domestic products and enrich the rural economy, the department has planned to organize a provincial native cloth roving exhibition. It is stipulated that the native cloth products sent by various counties should be gathered and exhibited in the provincial capital first, and then transported to the counties for roving exhibitions in turn, so as to learn from each other and improve. Three kinds of regulations and two kinds of forms have been formulated and submitted to the provincial government for record. It has been found that the county belongs to the cloth-producing area. In addition to separate orders, the regulations and forms of the provincial native cloth roving exhibition are hereby sent for compliance." The county government immediately transferred the order to the Zhuanqiao Agricultural Education Center and the Minhang and other three chambers of commerce for compliance.

Seedling Raising for National Salvation 150

— Zhan Lu

Ever since the September 18th Incident, the act of hanging up the banner of national salvation while secretly engaging in seedling raising has been played out many times behind the scenes. Recently, a young man surnamed Guo on the Xi'an ship traveling between Guangzhou and Hong Kong also tried this trick, but was unfortunately seen through and ultimately failed, which shows that the ancient saying "The more one tries to deceive, the more clumsy one becomes" is indeed of considerable value.

In early October, during the process of the Xi'an ship sailing from Hong Kong to Guangzhou, a young man surnamed Guo, who lived in room number 10 of the Western restaurant, displayed a kind of painful and dejected attitude, stepping over the ship's railing to seek a place to return to in the vast sea. The crew's rescue was quick, and he was not able to fall into the water. After various consolations from the crowd, Mr. Guo reluctantly returned to his room.

The rescued Mr. Guo deeply regretted not being able to die. Under the surveillance of his fellow passengers, he was also found to be hanging himself with a rope in his room. After the crowd took away the rope, Mr. Guo was still unable to die. The crowd was unable to guard against everything, and had no choice but to tie his hands and feet to prevent him from seeking death a third time.

According to Mr. Guo's statement: He is a student from Yunnan who was heartbroken by the fall of Dong Province and traveled a long distance to join the army, determined to fight the invaders to the death. He once served as a secretary for the volunteer army. Because our army was defeated under the enemy's air raids, he escaped from the tiger's mouth and drifted here, and he was so heartbroken by the national crisis that he would rather die.

After being passed on among the fellow passengers, it aroused a very warm sympathy from the crowd, and everyone wanted to contribute as much as they could to rescue this enthusiastic patriotic young man. However, one female passenger reported to the crowd that she had witnessed Mr. Guo performing the same act on the Zhongxing ship sailing from Macau to Hong Kong. Fellow passengers contributed as much as they could and gave him more than 40 yuan before he stopped seeking death. Today's action is just "following the example" and "doing the same thing again." After this report, Mr. Guo's seedling raising trick was declared a failure.

Seedling raising! Seedling raising! You have so many ways to cheat, why bother hanging up this banner of national salvation and affecting the genuine national salvation work of patriotic youth? Seedling raising! Seedling raising! I advise you not to hang up this banner in the future.

Live Head Cutting 151

— Ke Ding'an

｜Tragedy in the Countryside｜

The giant wheel of the times is moving forward relentlessly, and at the same time, it is sowing bad seeds in big cities and small villages. What I need to say now is about a fact in the countryside of nearby Wuxing County, which is indeed too tragic!

It should be said at the beginning that the protagonist of this tragedy - is really a supporting role. Generally, it is always the lower-class people, but sometimes there may be exceptions. What I know is that in the past, it was the local tyrants and evil gentry who dominated the locality in every village. Although the old tyrants and evil gentry have disappeared in form and shadow, the new tyrants and evil gentry, like bamboo shoots after rain, are constantly emerging, and at the same time, they are rampant with their tricks. The new tyrants and evil gentry, of course, have their minions like the old tyrants and evil gentry. These minions are the local hooligans. They are already doing all kinds of evil on weekdays, as long as they have money. Now that they have taken up the position of minions of the new tyrants and evil gentry, they are naturally even more eager to show their diligence.

The minions often pay attention to whether the lower-class people under their control have the opportunity to be blackmailed. For example, a strong man has just died in the ×× family, and there is only an old mother and wife in the house of the deceased. This is a good opportunity for the minions to arrive, and it can also be said that the financial army of the new tyrants and evil gentry is coming!

In the new tyrants and evil gentry's pockets, there are many lower-class people who want to marry cheap spouses. He uses the minions to run several times, and this poor widow falls into the arms of a hungry tiger. The price of this cheap spouse given by the other party varies depending on the beauty or ugliness of the widow's appearance. Generally, the best is 200 yuan, and the worst is no more than 100 yuan.

If the new tyrant and evil gentry determines that it is 200 yuan, then the widow's mother-in-law will get at most 50 yuan. The rest of the round number goes to the new tyrant and evil gentry, and the odd number is of course for the minions to squander.

The name of this tragedy is the shocking: "Live Head Cutting" three words! Perhaps the same tragedy is happening elsewhere, but its naming is different!

Scientific Anecdotes 152

— Gao Qian

｜Why Do Birds Know the Way?｜

Summer is gone, and every autumn, countless birds (such as swallows) fly from the north to the tropical countries in the south. This long-distance flight across the ocean is a very strange phenomenon. Because we humans must have skilled pilots to navigate, and we must also rely on nautical charts and compasses. Even with such thorough equipment, we sometimes make mistakes. As for birds, needless to say, they do not have so many instruments, and in the vast sea, there is nothing to eat, but they can fly thousands of miles. Isn't that the most bizarre thing? Of course, many birds die in the middle of the sea due to exhaustion, and the rest who reach their destination are also half-dead from hunger, but they can eventually reach their destination, which is always a strange thing.

How can birds recognize such a long journey? Biologists have not yet found a definite answer.

Generally speaking, we can guess that this is what the old birds teach the young birds. If people teach them, they can remember. We can say that birds have an extremely strong memory for this.

In addition, birds may have a strange sense of direction. We know that some people have difficulty recognizing roads, and some people can remember a place clearly after only walking there once. Perhaps birds are far superior to humans in this respect. If you blindfold a bird and spin it around a few times, it may know which way it is facing. We humans, on the other hand, if we are blindfolded and spun a few times, we will not know which direction we have spun to.

Heartfelt Words of a Chinese Technician 153

— Zeng Guang

｜A Word From Pan Yuzhen｜

Among the skill classes in our country, there are not many that can amaze people with their performances, have a large number of talents, and are famous abroad. The skill class led by Pan Yuzhen, a Chinese skill master, is one of them.

Mr. Pan had great ambitions since he was a child. He learned skills from famous teachers and practiced hard for ten years, and his skills greatly improved. When he grew up, he took his two sisters, Yulan and Yurong, and traveled across the oceans to various countries around the world, specializing in promoting Chinese martial arts abroad. Wherever he went, thousands of people were mobilized, but Mr. Pan never took this for granted.

Mr. Pan's two sisters are outstanding in appearance. Under the guidance of their brother, their martial arts are also very famous. They performed in Europe and the United States a few years ago, and as weak women, they performed martial arts that strong men could not do. No wonder people in Europe and the United States were amazed.

Mr. Pan not only takes it as his duty to promote national skills, but also his patriotism is no less than others. He is deeply pained by foreigners who mock our people as the sick men of East Asia. He once said to others, "The strength of a country always depends on the physical strength of the people as the standard. If the people's physical strength is healthy, then the country will never be rich and strong. Now, the people of our country do not seek the art of fitness, and they are extremely weak, to the point of being dying and incurable, and foreign insults are becoming more and more urgent. If we want to save China today, we should make it our urgent task to strengthen our physique."

Mr. Pan's skill class returned to the motherland from abroad yesterday and arrived in Shanghai. Also coming with him was Ms. Ju Ji, who was born with a singing voice and is the pillar of the most famous "Ziegfeld Follies" in the United States. Ms. Ju is the first Chinese girl to join the group and become a singer. It is said that Mr. Pan and others will lead the entire cast of artists from Shanghai to Europe next month.

Traitor's Mirror 154

— ·Nan· Gong

Since the September 18th Incident, the three eastern provinces have fallen entirely due to non-resistance. The people of the Northeast have suffered the trampling of the Japanese army. Those who have lost their minds and gone mad have become shameless, acting as accomplices of tigers, thinking that it is a shortcut to wealth and giving up the shame of slaves, serving the enemy. My friend Hutou, who wrote from Yuanning, was unable to bear the oppression of the Japanese, and wrote about the matter of a traitor. Hearing this, I was refreshed and quickly recorded it in this talk as a mirror for those who act as traitors.

Li, from Laizhou, Shandong, once served as a low-ranking officer in the Zhilu Army and was friendly with the traitor Jin Bogong. Jin is a member of the Banner people and is now serving as a bodyguard for Puyi in the puppet state. Li was overjoyed when he heard this and quickly packed his bags and went to the puppet state to see Jin and seek a job, thinking that since Jin was a bodyguard, he would see Puyi every morning and evening and it would not be difficult to get a position. He did not know that even Puyi, who was called the head of the state, did not have the power of an ordinary Japanese, let alone Jin? When Jin saw that Li had arrived, he recommended him to the puppet Ministry of Industry because he was unable to help. The minister was also surnamed Li, from Shandong. At that time, people were afraid of the devastation of the Japanese and were unwilling to be their puppets, and very few people went to be traitors. Seeing that Li had arrived, he treated him as a fellow villager and gave him the position of director. Li was overjoyed, thinking that he was climbing the ladder of success and would be rich and noble forever. Before a month had passed, the Japanese gradually revealed their hideous faces to the various ministries of the puppet state, wanting to seize real power. The Ministry of Industry was one of the ministries that they had to get in particular, because they had to seize all the mineral industries in the Northeast. They were also afraid that the international community would oppose them in the name of justice, so they did not dare to seize the position of minister immediately, but instead sought to replace all the directors with Japanese. Li was elated and completely unaware. One day, a Japanese named Tanaka visited Li and they had a pleasant conversation. Li wanted to make friends with the Japanese, so he would do his best to smile ingratiatingly when he saw them. Seeing Tanaka's visit, he thought it was an unusual honor and did his best to entertain him. Tanaka visited Li's residence every day and often boasted that he had a close relationship with Muto. Li was even more respectful. In less than half a month, one evening, Tanaka said to Li that he had been ordered by Muto to organize a plainclothes team and had become the commander-in-chief. He knew that Li was familiar with martial arts and hired him as the chief of staff, and he did not have to resign from his position as director. Li was overjoyed. Tanaka gave him two pistols and a symbol. Li accepted them without suspicion. From then on, Li boasted that he had gained the trust of the Japanese. A few days later, Tanaka said to Li, "I have recommended you to Muto. We will go to Shenyang to meet him tonight." Li did not think at all, dressed up, wore his gun, and went to Shenyang by car with Tanaka. When he arrived at Shenyang Station, Japanese soldiers came and questioned Li and searched his luggage. When they saw the pistol, they immediately handcuffed him and said that he was a spy for the guerrillas. At that time, Tanaka was standing by, saying nothing, waving his hand and ordering the soldiers to take Li away. In the evening, Li was interrogated at the police headquarters. He saw Tanaka whispering to the interrogator. Li cried for help, but the Japanese soldiers had already dragged him down the hall. With a loud bang, this traitor who dreamed of wealth and honor followed the ruthless bullets to the afterlife! It was all Tanaka's cunning plan. He killed Li with a pistol in order to seize the position of director. On the second day after Li went to Shenyang, the puppet Minister of Industry received an order from the Japanese, saying that Director Li was a guerrilla spy and had been executed, and Tanaka was appointed as the director. After the puppet minister saw the order, he knew the truth, but he did not dare to say anything.

Commercial News

Financial News: Gold Price Reaches a High of Eighteen Taels Last Week 156

｜Rising Momentum Accelerates Short Squeeze｜

Last week's bidding price for gold coincided with the swap period (ten sessions in January). The market trend was strong, although the initial state was mediocre, and trading in December was slow. As the swap approached, the price difference was only two or three taels. Subsequently, there was a rapid change, and a new high of over 760 taels was reached. Initially, the silver market was slightly different, and the exchange rate continued to rise, so the Shanghai market's sterling was tight. The December gold price opened high at 749.2 taels, an increase of 2.5 taels. There were also rumors that the United States opposed the extension of war debts, subsequently exceeding 50 taels. Furthermore, Reuters reported that India had a surplus of silver reserves and planned to sell them, which further strengthened the market. Later, the gold price advanced due to the contraction of the silver market and the frequent decline of the US dollar exchange rate. On Wednesday, it reached 755.8 taels, closing at 53.4 taels at noon. However, as the swap date approached, the market switched to January futures, opening at 747.5 taels (December 54 taels, a difference of 6.5 taels, indicating a premium for the long position). The price then briefly hovered around 47 taels. Since the market was closed on Wednesday, and the exchange rate fell again despite a stable silver market the next day, with the pound sterling firm and the US dollar strong, the gold price continued to rise, albeit slightly. On Friday, silver prices in the UK and the US diverged, and the exchange rate plummeted, resulting in a strong sterling and a brisk US dollar. Moreover, with vigorous buying from Guangbang, Hengxing, Yifeng, and various short sellers, it suddenly broke through the 60-tael mark. The morning market was therefore low, but at noon, news suddenly spread that the US budget deficit for next year would be excessive, potentially leading to a shift to the silver standard. This news caused a setback in confidence. In the afternoon, Hengyu replaced Hengxing to cover more than 4,000 short positions, reaching 62 taels. On Saturday, the rising trend slowed slightly. The pound sterling remained unchanged, and the US dollar fell slightly, but the exchange rate suddenly turned upward, opening low. Subsequently, there was not much prosperity or decline, and the price returned within 60 taels, closing at 58.7 taels. Taking into account the previous Saturday (plus the swap, estimated at about 6 taels), the increase was 18 taels, with a full-week review of 15 taels (the difference between the opening and closing prices was 11.2 taels). The January contract has risen for two weeks, totaling about 20 taels. As for the swap, it was pre-arranged at 3.4 or 3.5 taels on the 15th, and formal trading began the next day, estimated at around 5 taels. Subsequently, it was quoted above 7 taels, but the exchange traded at 6.5 taels, then around 6 taels. On Saturday, it was between 6.8 or 6.9 taels to 6.4 taels. However, Hengxing's short positions were still not fully covered, and the January positions were largely filled, almost breaking even, suggesting a potential shift to a long position. Dalianbang, Yifeng, Yongqian, Changxiang, Yuanheng, and other long positions took advantage of the momentum and began to exit their positions. Overseas silver markets contracted slightly, and the local exchange market saw parity between sterling and gold, with the US dollar quoted at a small 0.25 discount, while the internal market generally contracted by half a point (0.125 for sterling, 0.25 for the US dollar). Because exchange rate fluctuations were uneven, the trends diverged significantly. Chinese gold firms such as Zhonghua and Dalianbang/Guangbang all covered short positions. Because the bidding price of gold increased more and more powerfully, the hedging values increased, and the hedging price was initially pressed at 60-70 taels, then calculated within 60 taels, ultimately over 60 taels. Initially, exchange rose then dropped, ultimately rebounding. The total change was smaller than the prior week. The pound fell against the US dollar by 2.25, and the US dollar fell against the pound by 2.375. The high and low prices of silver prices and exchange rates are listed below:

Category Highest Lowest Change from Previous Saturday

Fragmented Money Market Quiet on Sundays 157

Yesterday was another Sunday, a day when banks are closed and the market was quiet. The market price of foreign currency for silver was 7 mace, 1 fen, 1 li, 7 hao, 5 si in the morning session, and 7 mace, 1 fen, 1 li, 8 hao, 7 si, 5 hu in the afternoon session. The amount of remittance drafts made was only 320,000 in the morning session and only 330,000 in the afternoon session. Banknotes were 20,000 in the morning session and 40,000 in the afternoon session. There were no reports of banknotes on the unofficial market. Securities: 19th Customs Bonds Continue to Rise by Two Yuan 159

｜Other Bonds Also Increase by Varying Amounts of One Yuan and Several Jiao｜

｜Market Conditions Are Slightly Clear, with Transactions Reaching 29 Million｜

Over the past week (from November 14th to 19th), the market conditions for various bonds on the Chinese Securities Exchange were extremely clear. The spot market saw only 100,220 yuan in transactions, with 20,000 yuan accounted for by old tickets of the 1986 Public Bonds, 13,000 to 14,000 yuan each for Abolishment and Salt Tax Bonds, and 7,000 to 8,000 yuan for other bonds. The futures market was also far inferior to the previous week. The market was characterized by stable prices and a calm atmosphere, no longer as lively as the previous week. An examination of the daily transaction situation reveals that Thursday was the most active, with approximately 7.2 million, and Friday was relatively clear, with over 3.1 million. The remaining days were between 4 and 5 million yuan. The total was 29.6 million, a decrease of over 20.4 million yuan compared to the previous week, including 2.47 million for the November Salt Tax Bonds, 3.95 million for the December Salt Tax Bonds, 2.435 million for the November Consolidated Tax Bonds, 3.04 million for the December Consolidated Tax Bonds, 2.16 million for the November 20th Customs Bonds, 2.185 million for the December 20th Customs Bonds, 1.555 million for the November 20th Rolled Bonds, 1.69 million for the December 20th Rolled Bonds, 1.64 million for the November Disbandment Bonds, 1.585 million for the December Disbandment Bonds, 1.29 million for the November 19th Customs Bonds, 955,000 for the December 19th Customs Bonds, 1.095 million for the November 19th Philanthropy Bonds, 955,000 for the December 19th Philanthropy Bonds, 1.33 million for the November Abolishment Bonds, 480,000 for the December Abolishment Bonds, and other bonds only opened for the November term, including 405,000 yuan for Customs Duties, 200,000 yuan for Restructuring 6% Bonds, 175,000 yuan for 1986 Public Bonds, and 5,000 yuan for Financial Bonds. An examination of the forward trading of various bonds shows that as the end of the month approaches, trading is quite active. In the past week, it has exceeded the recent trading. As for the trends of various bond prices in the past week, the domestic and international situation has been very calm, and there have been no new developments in the bond market environment. Although the buying interest in the market is still good, the major players are adopting a wait-and-see attitude. The market is different from before. The rising momentum of bond prices seems to have come to an end in the previous week. Although the prices have generally continued to rise, the trend is moderate and far from the frequent major ups and downs of the previous week. An examination of the daily changes in the past week shows that Monday was the strongest, with gains of 7-8 jiao to one yuan or several jiao. The buying interest was also the strongest. Tuesday saw a slight reaction, around half a yuan. The daily gains were steady between Wednesday and Thursday, but the fluctuations were minimal, only two or three jiao to half a yuan each day. Friday saw a slight contraction, and Saturday turned upward again. The stable situation remained unchanged from before. Although market trading was not quiet in the past week, the approaching end of the month led to an increase in swap transactions, and the supply and demand situation was balanced. As a result, compared to the previous week, only the 19th Philanthropy futures continued to rise by two yuan, while most other futures rose by one yuan to one yuan and five or six jiao. Only the Restructuring 6% and Financial Bonds fell slightly. Judging from the bond market situation, it seems optimistic. However, in the near term, as the settlement approaches, it is feared that the market will remain stable and not experience major ups and downs. Cotton Yarn Market Report for the Week 160

｜People give up, demand falls, sales plummet｜

Over the past week, the cotton yarn market has continued to decline, with each day seeming worse than the last. Due to the poor environment, there has been a need for stagnation. All sectors have no hope of development. The Sichuan war has not ended, the financial situation is urgent, and as a result, commercial depression is unbearable. Inquiries reveal that daily transactions in the spot yarn market have only been three or four hundred to two or three hundred bales. Under these circumstances, how can the market be sustained? Therefore, although the Yong'an Factory is struggling to maintain a long position, the trend is such that the decline is difficult to reverse. As for the overseas cotton industry, it is also in a state of fatigue and sluggishness, so most speculators are leaning towards the short side. The monthly price broke through the 40-tael mark, reaching a low of 39.3 taels. Inquiries reveal that the lowest price in mid-June of this year was 138.4 taels, a difference of only 9 qian. Most targets are looking for a new low below the price of 38.4 taels. In short, judging from the general trend, the situation is extremely pessimistic. Inquiries reveal that the total amount of cotton yarn purchased by various sectors throughout the week was 5,358 bales, of which 25 bales were goods opened by the Shenxin Factory, all of which were accepted by speculators. The spot price of opened yarn has fallen by about 2 taels. The bidding price of yarn in the near month has fallen by 2.4 qian compared to the previous week, and the far month has fallen by 9 qian to 1.5 taels. The total turnover for the week was 159,300 bales. The purchase amount of each sector is listed below:

Cotton Market: Actual Position Strengthened Last Week 161

｜Inversely Proportional to the Yarn Market｜

Spot Market Demand Also Good

Over the past week, although the cotton market has softened in appearance, it has actually been exceptionally strong. However, the situation in the US cotton market is also one of consolidation. Although some manufacturers have been selling large quantities of standard cotton, the pressure has been heavy. However, the delivery deadline for this month is approaching, and the supply from various sources remains scarce. Moreover, the prices in various producing areas are difficult to loosen. Given the situation in various places, it is more cost-effective to buy in the futures market to offset short positions. Therefore, purchases were made on [date] of this month to cover short positions, and the market rose, in inverse proportion to the yarn market. The spot cotton business in the market is still good. The cotton market is more expensive than the yarn market, but the overseas cotton industry is still in a slump. The future of the cotton market is uncertain. The source of cotton is calculated as 3,803 bales of Yao cotton and 8,333 bales of cotton. The total turnover of standard cotton for the week was 310,600 bales. The prices for each month are near month, up 4.7 qian from the previous week, and far month, up 2.3 qian. US cotton fell by 30 points compared to the previous week. Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

The Words of a Villager 175

— Buddha

Yesterday, a fellow villager came to see me. He was already over fifty years old, so I had no choice but to entertain him. He talked incessantly, starting with a major robbery that had occurred in the home of a certain surname in the east village, then about the son of a cousin in the west village who, at twenty-one years old, still couldn't walk, and finally about the difficulties of the seven daily necessities these days.

He said that when he was young, the price of rice was measured in foreign sacks (i.e., two dollars per picul), and all kinds of goods were very cheap, so life was exceptionally good. Compared to the current cost of living, it had increased about tenfold. Some things were certainly not as bad, but others were even worse. When he was a child, a haircut cost only sixteen cash, or at most twenty cash, but now a haircut costs twenty or thirty cents. He had heard that some cost seventy or eighty cents, or even a dollar. He asked how many times the price had increased. Therefore, life now is truly difficult.

I said that villagers like him were alright, and as the saying goes, "A city dweller is impoverished by a drop of soy sauce, while a villager is impoverished by an iron crutch." He said that was exactly the point, that the villagers were left with no means of survival. The prices of all goods had increased tenfold or more, while the price of rice was getting worse and worse, almost to the point of being worthless. Who would want to farm then? He had heard that things were already like this in Hunan and other places, where each picul of rice was only selling for two dollars and forty cents. He asked how such a life could be considered livable.

I asked him why the price of rice was so high. He said that he didn't know, but he had heard people say that this year was originally a year of abundance everywhere, but the heavy taxes levied everywhere made it impossible for rice to circulate. In particular, some knowledgeable people had borrowed a large amount of American wheat to bring in. He had heard that the first batch had already arrived, and there were second and third batches coming. He asked if the price of rice could still rise.

I laughed and said to him that he truly didn't know his blessings. It was a blessing for him, but he was worried. The people of our country were inherently blessed. They didn't have to do anything or move at all, and everything would be sent to them to enjoy. I asked if there was anything among the clothes, utensils, etc., that people in our country had to make themselves. We only had to take out money, and there was nothing we couldn't get. Even guns and cannons could be bought from other countries and used to kill each other. Our country was originally founded on agriculture, and it was the villagers who suffered the most. They had not yet received a proper amount of happiness. Now that batches of grain were coming in, they could eat without plowing and wear clothes without weaving. This was their blessing. Did they even know it?

The villager realized that there was no point in talking to me, so he took his leave. I also made a note of this for the sake of providing talking points.

Science

Method of Manufacturing Calcium Carbide 178

— Zhong Rong

When evening comes, one sees the calcium carbide lamps on package cars and free cars, which are brightly delightful. However, they are imported goods and are very expensive, not worthwhile. Now, the raw materials for calcium carbide and the manufacturing procedure are written below for the sake of imitation by the countrymen in order to avoid the outflow of profit rights.

(1) Raw Materials: The raw materials needed for manufacturing calcium carbide are quicklime (i.e., calcium oxide, also known as calcium oxide) and anthracite coal. The quicklime must be fresh and not contain moisture, because if it contains too much moisture, it will generate excessive heat and turn into slaked lime. Slaked lime is not a suitable raw material for manufacturing calcium carbide. Anthracite coal should also be selected for its purity and quality. After mixing the raw materials, it is best to manufacture them directly. If the mixture is placed in a humid place, the amount should be reduced. Care should be taken during manufacturing.

(2) Manufacturing Method: The manufacturing method is divided into grinding, mixing, drying, calcination, and condensation. The processes are described in order below.

Page 17

A. Grinding: The selected raw materials are separately put into a grinding machine (or a stone mortar can be used instead, as long as the purpose of grinding is achieved). Grind into extremely fine powder and place in another container. Then, sift through a fine silk sieve to remove impurities (such as sand, stones, and soil). After the impurities are sifted out, they can be mixed.

B. Mixing: Mixing involves mixing quicklime and anthracite coal. The amount to be mixed depends on the composition of the raw materials. Approximately 28 parts of quicklime powder and 18 parts of anthracite coal powder are used. After mixing, stir with a rod until the mixture is thoroughly uniform, then dry it.

C. Drying: Spread the raw materials evenly on a white cloth and dry in the sun. If artificial drying is used, the room temperature should be around 80 degrees.

D. Calcination: Calcination involves placing the dried raw materials in an electric furnace and gradually calcining them. When calcined to white heat, they emit calcium oxide gas. The calcium carbide obtained in this way does not yield good results, so condensation is performed again.

E. Condensation: After calcination is complete, the calcium carbide is poured out and transferred to a cooling tank (the cooling tank should be made of iron, shaped like a common household clothing box. The inside of the tank should be smooth, and a little oil should be dripped into the tank and wiped clean with a dry cloth to prevent corrosion). Allow it to condense. If you want to make it into a square or round shape, you must pour it into an iron mold (the mold must be wiped clean) to wait for condensation, and then the calcium carbide is formed.

(Note) Calcium carbide should be wrapped in cloth (or thick paper can be used instead) and placed in a desiccant for long-term storage. Take it out when using it.

Remembering Past Battles 179

— Kang Shi

Since the Songkou Fort has been closed to visitors, those who come to the Songhu Road to remember the battles are filled with a sense of vicissitudes. On the morning of the ninth, I, along with two friends, Lin and Zhou, made a trip to remember the past battles. I will record the scenery along the way as follows:

When the train passed the Tiantong'an Station, Japanese soldiers with guns and equipment were patrolling at the end of North Sichuan Road. Their arrogant attitude caused those who witnessed it in the same car to be filled with anger. As the car passed Zhabei, a scene of scorched earth moved them. Alas! The people's morale is like this, but what about the weakness of those in power?

Before long, we arrived in front of the embankment of the Fort Command, where we saw a wooden sign with the words "By Order, No Visitors Allowed - Fort Management Office." The embankment was also cut off to prevent visitors, and a policeman was stationed there to guard it, which was very careful. We went around to the left side of the fort, but were blocked by barbed wire. Just as we were feeling frustrated, we suddenly saw a canvas shoe worn by a soldier, sinking into the roadside for about an inch. We couldn't help but sigh repeatedly. We secretly speculated that the owner of the shoe might have sacrificed to defend the territory, and left the shoe behind to warn future generations. However, in the present day, things have changed, and few people ask about it. Isn't it painful!

The platforms of stations such as Fort Taiwan are all riddled with bullets, so the tops of the platforms are like beehives, and many of the cement columns are broken in the middle. They have not been repaired to this day, and the desolate scene fills one with endless sadness! As the car passed various places, we saw that the houses of the people that had been bombed had all become open-air houses, with only the surrounding walls remaining and no roofs. How miserable! How painful! However, even after suffering such a great disaster at the hands of the tyrannical Japanese, there are still those who are willing to be traitors and merchants. It is truly incomprehensible.

Ten Commandments for Traveling 180

— Li Huo

(1) If you have not been to a place and need to ask for directions, you can inquire at old shops or from older people. Because they have lived there for a long time, they are naturally familiar with the geography. When inquiring, you must be sincere and polite, and not arrogant or rude. Otherwise, you will be tricked, and others will point you in all directions, causing you to walk around aimlessly, never reaching your destination.

(2) When taking a tram, if you have important items, you can put them in the inside pocket on your left side, put your left hand down to press on them, and use your right hand to hold onto the ring. Be calm. If someone you don't know strikes up a conversation with you, don't respond to them. Otherwise, you will be distracted and forget your things, and they will end up in their pockets.

(3) If you hear gunfire on the street, it is best to hide in a nearby shop. Do not panic and run around frantically. The police will think you are a thief, and you may be hit by a stray bullet.

(4) If you encounter a search on the street, you must raise both hands high and allow them to search you. The most important thing to avoid is putting your hands in your pockets. Do not think that you have money on you and quickly reach into your pocket to hold it tight. If the police see this, they will mistakenly think you are holding a gun, and a dangerous situation may occur.

(5) If you see someone drop a leather item or package on the street, do not be greedy and pick it up. Otherwise, someone will testify against you and extort money, saying that you stole it. If you look inside the leather item and see that it is full of paper, they will extort ten or eight dollars from you.

(6) If you have three rickshaws full of things and you can only sit in one yourself, then it is not easy to take care of the other two. You can write down the registration numbers of the other two rickshaws. If something unexpected happens, you can report it to the police station for investigation.

(7) If you are holding something in your hands, do not look at the items displayed in shop windows. If you are absorbed in looking at something, it will be an opportunity for petty thieves to strike.

(8) The goods hawked on the street may seem very cheap, but once you buy them and use them, they will have defects. Therefore, no matter how cheap something is, it is best not to buy it, so as not to be deceived.

(9) Rickshaw parking areas are often located on small roads and open spaces. If you come out of a major company or movie theater, you should be willing to walk a few more steps to a small road to hire one. The price will be fair. Otherwise, you will be ripped off.

(10) If you are returning from a movie theater or amusement park at 12 o'clock at night and passing through deserted roads, it is better to call for a rickshaw or take a longer route through lively areas, because at that time of night, there are very few pedestrians. If you encounter robbers, you will be threatened.

In the Tram 181

— Wu

Yesterday, when I stepped onto a tram on Route 1, I felt truly fortunate, because I had never ridden on such a spacious tram before. In the large carriage, there were only three people in total, including myself. Therefore, I boldly relaxed my joints and sat on the chair, able to put on the airs of riding in a private car. At this time, I could pay attention to the conversation of the other two, because I had a free mind.

Their conversation had been going on for a long time, but the burly, great gentleman wearing a robe of patterned silk was very excited. He said to the short man with a mustache that could almost be counted below his nose:

"Ah! My happy days are completely over!"

I could tell that this was a Sichuan accent. The other party continued, saying:

"But you don't have to be pessimistic. Maybe you will have good luck later. Who knows what will happen in the future?"

A flattering smile was offered before the big man's eyes, but the big man did not seem to pay attention, perhaps he was still deep in his own sighs. Soon, he said again:

"From the age of eighteen until eight years ago, I never left my post. I had food to eat and things to use. I certainly had some good days, but these past eight years have been impossible. Ah!"

"Yes, yes, the so-called noble people suffer a lot! Haha! But I think you must have saved up a lot of money, right?"

"Money? Don't even mention it. If I had been willing to make money back then, needless to say, I would have had hundreds of thousands by now. But at that time, I always followed my father's words, 'A civil official does not love money, a military official is not afraid of death.' Even if the money was right in front of my eyes, I was not willing to take it, so I am still penniless."

"Yes, yes. If all the military officers in China were like you, that would be great. But you should have saved some money for retirement, sir, do you agree? May I ask, I think you must still have tens of thousands of dollars in savings, right?"

"Hmph, I still have some money for pocket money, otherwise, I wouldn't have been able to do nothing for the past eight years. What would I have used?"

"Oh, oh, oh! Yes, yes. As long as you can get by, that's enough."

"But how can this little bit of money be enough? Although there are not many people, it costs money to maintain two mansions, one large and one small, in Shanghai."

When I heard this, I immediately imagined his power when he was in office, and the happiness of having a house full of wives and concubines. But according to him, this was still a time of bad luck. Otherwise, coming out for a walk would not have required taking the tram, and he would at least be in an Austin.

At this time, I saw that the man with the small mustache took out a rubber-tipped cigarette and offered it to the man in the patterned silk robe, and respectfully struck a match for him. This made me even more interested. Later, the man with the small mustache said again:

"I heard that Division Commander Liu is going to rely on you again."

"That's just him joking with me. Do you think I would take on a nominal advisor role? You have to know that if you want to be an official, you must have troops. With an army, everything is easy to say. Without military power, it's better not to do it. But is Division Commander Liu willing to let me command troops? He knows he can't control me, so he's giving me a useless title to collect a salary."

"But since Division Commander Liu treats you so well, I think you should condescend a little."

"I can't do that. When I was a regimental commander, he was just a regimental commander. Now he wants me to condescend to him? That's a joke."

"That's true, but if you go, it would be a great help to me, right? Surely you wouldn't be unwilling to get me a small job, sir? Hahaha!"

They both laughed unnaturally.

Unfortunately, I had arrived at my stop, so I had to get off. I don't know what happened after that.

My heart felt heavy. I thought that these two were both talents from Sichuan. Perhaps it was because Sichuan's mountains and rivers were so spiritual that so many talents came out, which is why there are so many endless tragedies of bloodshed today.

A Terrifying Night 182

— Yichen

About two months ago, a family moved into the house across from my window. The female homeowner was a beautiful and fashionable young lady. Her husband, although not riding a jade-bridled horse or eating carp from a golden plate, seemed to have some wealth in my eyes. An exquisite Austin and a beautiful wife had long aroused my jealousy and envy, so I had to sigh at their happiness!

However, I paid such attention to them because their movements seemed a bit mysterious. Yes! Returning home at two o'clock in the middle of the night and going out at three or four o'clock in the afternoon couldn't help but arouse suspicion, could it?

A half-moon hung in the sky, and sparse stars dotted the sky, dancing in an instant. Apart from the barking of dogs in the distance, there was no other sound. It was a gentle and beautiful night, but the incident also occurred on this night, this gentle and beautiful night.

Normally, I would sleep soundly until dawn, but today was different. I tossed and turned, unable to fall asleep. Suddenly, a horn broke the silence, shaking my eardrums. "Yes! Since I can't sleep, why not get up and take a look at that beauty!" Before I had finished thinking this, my body had involuntarily wandered to the window!

Although I had sometimes seen them come back, there was an additional young man in a suit today! No! Maybe he comes often, because I haven't gotten up to peek these past few nights, so this time I'm even more suspicious. I leaned on the window sill and watched them open the door, close the door, go to the parlor, go upstairs...

Unfortunately, the pink curtains blocked my view, but I couldn't block my hearing. Laughter, singing, and talking constantly rippled over. I stared blankly at the shadows of the people reflected from behind the curtains. The clock chimed! Ding! Ding! Ding! Ding! It had already struck four!

Ah! Something's not right. Half an hour later, their movements were a little off. Why were the dark shadows moving back and forth so busily? Ah! Isn't that a knife in the shadow's hand? Alas! What did he fall over! ... Then there was a sound of overturned bowls, tables, and chairs.

"Ooh..." The man in the suit and the young lady grabbed a package and hurriedly rushed downstairs, opened the car, and left!

Shivers, fear, and dread, layer upon layer of hot blood rushed to my heart. "Sleep Demons" had long flown to the ninth heaven. Before long, the sky was faintly bright, and a noisy sound filled the alley.

"Terrible! The young master... is dead... dead! Grandma! Where... where did they go! ...""I'm going to report it!" "The police are here? ... Ah! The big shots are here too!" "A body in a pool of blood... a knife...?"

I, who was across the window, was shaking even more violently, almost with my knees rubbing against the floor! "Jealousy! Lust! Greed!" kept swirling in my mind.

International News

The Organization of the Soviet Film Company 184

—

The Soviet Film Company was founded in 1925, abbreviated as Sovkino (Cobknbo). In addition to having the exclusive right to produce Soviet films, it also has the exclusive right to export and import films in the Soviet Union.

The shareholders of the Soviet Film Company are the founders of the company, namely the People's Education Committee, the Industrial Economic Council, the Moscow Soviet, the Leningrad Soviet, and the Commercial Committee. The company is organized into a management committee of eleven people, and the chairman is the secretary of the Central Committee of the Communist Party.

Five people are elected by the general meeting of shareholders to form a supervisory committee, one as the supervisor of the Moscow studio, one as the supervisor of the Leningrad studio, one as the supervisor of the promotion department, and one as the supervisor of the technology department.

Sovkino invested 5 million rubles in film production in the 1930 fiscal year, with the content distributed as follows: 40 artistic films, 30 newsreels, and 50 educational popularization and other miscellaneous films.

In the two studios in Moscow and Leningrad, 45 directors are employed, mainly Eisenstein, Romm, Kuleshov, Tallett, Vakhatov, Popov, and Torauberke.

The internal equipment of the company is also very complete, with research institutes for testing, an actor's club that can accommodate 340 people, a small dining room that can accommodate 200 people, a large dining room that can accommodate 1,200 people, two libraries (one general and one for personal use), a physical training center that can accommodate 100 people, bathhouses, studios, warehouses, and a hotel that can accommodate 500 people and can be immediately converted into a theater. In addition, there are well-equipped buildings such as sick rooms, sanatoriums, and meeting places for Communist Party members and Young Pioneers. Because the Soviet film industry is operated by the state, the socialistization of film companies is an inevitable trend.

Film Talk

Hell's Headquarters 186

— Yan Nan

Hunting films have been widely welcomed and praised in the past year, so the number of them produced in response to the trend is considerable. Today's new film showing at the New Light, Hell's Headquarters, is another film calling itself a hunting film.

Universal Pictures is the most active in producing this type of film, but this one cannot really be considered a masterpiece of Universal's beast films!

The actors are quite good: Jack Mulhall, though not robust enough, is still competent; the female lead, Barbara Weeks, gives a good performance; it is rare to see a female star filming amidst a group of wild beasts like this. Frank Mayo is commendable, especially in the scene where he is devoured by a lion.

The director is skillful in the way he shoots the scenes and their placement, and the scenery is also very good. Of course, this film has very few interior scenes; the magnificence of the exterior scenes adds much color to the film.

The plot is very convoluted, but unfortunately, many scenes that could have expressed emotion in the first half are omitted, and explained through dialogue. This inevitably makes it difficult for those with a limited grasp of English to fully understand, although the pronunciation is very clear.

Also, although the beast scenes are very exciting, there are too few of them, so that the audience cannot get the great terror and stimulation they hoped for!

It also clearly states that white people treat black slaves unequally and inhumanely. It also tells us about the effectiveness of conquering people with force versus conquering them with virtue.

An average comparison: This film is not as good as "Ingagi" and "Tarzan the Ape Man," but it is much better than "Little People of Africa" and "The Big Trail." It is entirely a love story, with a few African Congo landscapes and wild animals interspersed, forming the key to the ending. But the large quantity of ivory that is never seen is the center of the drama. Its strength lies in this; its weakness also lies in this.

Behind-the-Scenes of Filming Hell's Headquarters 187

— He

During the filming of a wild scene in Hell's Headquarters, Barbara Weeks was injured by an enraged leopard.

This unfortunate incident occurred after Barbara Weeks had just finished filming a scene with a trained leopard. But as she walked past the leopard after finishing the scene, the unreasonable beast suddenly leapt up, with its sharp claws outstretched, and pounced straight at Barbara Weeks. After Jack Mulhall's struggle, he finally managed to drive away the ferocious, angry leopard. However, the claw marks of thirteen bloody scratches were deeply engraved on Barbara Weeks' beautiful, fair legs!

Later, after Barbara Weeks rested in the hospital for several days, she continued filming the last and most exciting scenes with the leopard that had injured her!

General Opinion

The Question of Kisses in Domestic Films 188

— Hui Zun

The thing that makes us feel most unsatisfied when we watch foreign films and domestic films is the depiction of kisses. In foreign films, we often see four hot lips pressed tightly together, while in domestic films, we hardly ever see such kisses; at most, they use various methods to indicate a kiss.

At the most intense moments of love, or when passion is at its peak, I dare say that, apart from a passionate, wild kiss, there is no other way on the screen to express it fully. Let us think about it, how tense are our heartstrings when we see a deep kiss in a foreign film! And how unsatisfied and anticlimactic do we feel when we see the scenery suddenly change or a back view used when a kiss is about to happen in a domestic film!

Here, the question of kisses may not be a big deal for male stars, but the problem lies with the female stars. Perhaps, Western and Chinese customs are different. In foreign countries, kissing is a common thing, so it is easy to perform a kiss on the screen. But in China, kissing is done in private, a privilege reserved for lovers. Therefore, the female stars' fragrant lips are unwilling to be offered to the fake lovers on the screen.

In fact, film is a great art, and the most important condition of art is to reflect life. Who in life does not kiss their lover? Since life is like this, then the lovers on the screen should also kiss each other heartily, regardless of whether they are real lovers in reality or completely unrelated.

Therefore, female stars should sacrifice for the sake of great art. Sacrificing a kiss for art is much more valuable than a kiss secretly given to a lover behind people's backs.

Therefore, one should not act in a passionate film if one is unwilling to perform it!!

"The passionate kiss"

Star Biography

The Autobiography of Janet Gaynor, Part 1 189

— Bing

I was born on October 6, 1906, in Philadelphia. My father passed away when I was young. My stepfather, named Jones, was an electrician. He hoped from the time I was little that I would work in film. So my entry into the film industry was entirely due to his encouragement and guidance.

After I left school, I decided to look for work. One morning, I went to look for a job with a friend. Luckily, I found a job in a shoe store, earning $18 a week. But I soon became unemployed again. So I went back to school. At that time, my family moved from San Francisco to Los Angeles. I was very excited at this time, because I saw several big stars in that huge car, and I was extremely envious.

I first stepped onto a film set on a Christmas night, when I was working as an extra. But I was very enthusiastic and felt that life was not as monotonous as it was in school. After that, I joined Poverty Row Studios, taking on slightly more important roles. I gained valuable experience in these many ordinary films.

One day, Fox Studios was recruiting actresses. I applied. Unfortunately, the director chose a very experienced one. Perhaps the director was right, but at that time it was a huge blow to me.

Just when I was at Hal Roach Studios, I received a call from Fred Dating of Universal Studios, asking me to play an important leading role. After the success of this film, I went from being an extra to signing a contract with the company. (To be continued)

Local News

The Dawn of Air Freight for Domestic Films: "A Fate in Tears and Laughter" Flies Between Shanghai and Hankou 190

— Mei Lang

A film is shown simultaneously in two or more theaters in the same area. Newspapers carry large advertisements proclaiming "Simultaneous Premiere at Several Major Theaters," using this to create momentum and attract audiences. This is a relatively progressive business method that has become popular in the film industry recently. However, in reality, the key to achieving good results still depends on the quality of the film's content.

The multi-episode feature film "A Fate in Tears and Laughter" by Star Film Company is now being shown simultaneously in several major theaters, with Episodes One, Two, Three, and Four being released in quick succession. This is happening not only in Shanghai but also in theaters in Beijing, Hankou, Tianjin, and other places. For a time, demand exceeded supply, and even with many copies, there were still not enough to distribute. Therefore, when showing simultaneously in several theaters in one location, they came up with a method of sharing one copy among several theaters. They determined the times in advance. Theater A would start the screening on time. But as soon as one reel was finished, a designated person would immediately deliver it to Theaters B and C.

While "A Fate in Tears and Laughter" is being shown competitively in various locations, they have been using airmail planes to transport the film to and from Hankou in the past few days. It is said that the air freight rate for a one-way trip between Shanghai and Hankou is $2.90 per pound. Each film weighs approximately 60 pounds or more. The cost of shipping one time is calculated to be over 200 yuan. Although the sum is not small, it greatly shortens the distance and is extremely convenient. This "A Fate in Tears and Laughter" is the first time that a domestic film has been transported by airplane for business purposes. It will be a minor anecdote in film history.

Zasu Pitts, nicknamed the "Female Chaplin of Hollywood," is currently an actress at Paramount Pictures. She has been with Paramount for many years, and her weekly salary is 3,000 gold dollars. Perhaps she can get an even higher salary than 3,000 gold dollars.

Sensitive Audiences 192

— Ying

These days, there are many good films showing in Shanghai theaters. Yesterday, a reporter happened to visit two so-called second-class movie theaters. Unexpectedly, the compensation I received was beyond my initial expectations. I saw that the general audience, including myself, could be deeply moved. This also proves that these two films do have touching qualities.

The first is "The Phantom of the Opera," which is showing in Beijing. This film was originally a work by Lon Chaney from ten years ago, but it has recently been dubbed. However, when the Phantom appeared, a natural atmosphere of terror filled the entire theater. Many people, like the female character in the film, simultaneously cried out "Ah!" Because it was a night show, many timid people (mostly women) left their seats one after another. Isn't that strange?

The second is "Traces of the Orchid Valley," which is showing at the Central Theater. Of course, most of the people who go to the Central Theater are of the older (?) generation, and modern men and women rarely visit. So when "Traces of the Orchid Valley" first premiered at the New Light, there was no shortage of whispered conversations, but yesterday at the Central, the atmosphere was gloomy and miserable, and the sound of sobbing could be heard everywhere. This sound, of course, was not from the sound film. Even when leaving the theater, many people covered their eyes as they walked. If you look closely, seven or eight out of ten people have red tear streaks on their faces!

Film Treatise

The Motivating Force of Expression 193

— Chen Dabe

After practicing concentration a couple of times, you will feel that your breathing is subjected to a very strange pressure during practice. The higher the degree of concentration, the easier it is for you to feel your breathing. People who have never practiced various breathing exercises often feel short of breath, or even breathless.

This is the inevitable result of practicing expression. Working on a screen play is like working on a stage play. One hour of work often consumes several times more energy than other mental or physical work. This is because when we perform in the face of tense, ever-changing emotions, we expend too much energy, so we are very easily tired afterwards. Anyone who has filmed one or two expressive shots on a film set has experienced this unusually exhausting taste. People who are not physically sound or have problems with their respiratory organs have no connection with the camera, and that is the reason why.

Yes. Changes in emotions must be helped by deep breathing. Someone once asked me what the motivating force of expression is. I said that breathing is the motivating force of expression. No matter what expression you want to make, you must first adjust your respiratory system to exactly match the needs of that emotion in order to express it appropriately. Otherwise, no matter what expression you make, you will not be able to make it look exactly like the real thing. We see that the expressions in many domestic films are very naive and laughable, because people who have seized the status of stars through money, backing, relatives, changed love, and other improper means have never known that the central organ or motivating force of expression lies in breathing. In other words, the reason why many friends who are accustomed to watching imported films do not like to watch domestic films is because many stars have not yet known this "secret" of expression.
